Current Commentary

On the Influence of the Franco-Italian Rapprochement by Heng

After the Great War, France seemed to regard itself as the leader on the European continent. Although Italy was also part of the Entente, the various verbal promises made by Britain and France at the time to persuade it to join the Entente were barely fulfilled. As a result of its frustration, it was filled with resentment and could not help but feel jealous of France's position. Its ambition to peer into the Balkans and vie for Central Europe was also barely restrained. Therefore, in any setting, it often clashed with France. Notable examples include frequently courting Romania, a friend of France, in the hope of cooperation, and colluding with Germany, a historical enemy of France, to plot against France. Even its recent relationship with Hungary, initially, was not aimed at countering the Little Entente under the Versailles system. It was only after discovering Hitler's ambitions for Austria that it was arranged to be a vanguard against Germany. Therefore, the conflict between France and Italy has not only been long-standing, but the rift has also been deep. The fact that they can now abandon their past grievances and cooperate cannot be said to be a major shift in international relations.

The cooperation between France and Italy began last summer when Germany annexed Austria. Therefore, the process of its brewing has not been a matter of a day or two. However, it almost came to a halt after the Marseille incident. Ultimately, due to the sincerity of both France and Italy, the opportunity for cooperation was not extinguished. Secret negotiations have been underway for the past few months. However, given the complexity of the two countries' past relations and the differences in their aspirations, it is indeed difficult to reach a compromise. Therefore, Laval's trip to Rome was repeatedly postponed. Now that Laval has made the trip, there should be no major obstacles to the progress of the Franco-Italian negotiations.

What is the content of Franco-Italian cooperation? So far, there is little accurate information. Both countries are keeping it a secret and do not want to reveal anything. Therefore, whether what has been reported is reliable remains to be seen in the future. However, according to our speculation, the important issues between France and Italy are nothing more than four points: (1) The redistribution of North African colonies. (2) Guaranteeing the independence of Austria. (3) Revision of the Treaty of Versailles. (4) Naval equality. On these issues, France and Italy clearly have different positions. It is worthy of pondering what kind of approach will be taken to reach a compromise. According to recent European news, both France and Italy are shelving the issue of Franco-Italian naval equality, probably due to concessions from the Italian side. At the same time, France has conditionally accepted the proposal to revise the treaties of Central Europe, meaning that France is willing to consider any revision proposal that does not use violence. This is another indication of France's concession. As for the issue of Austrian independence, we have heard American newspapers claiming that Italy hopes that all related countries will jointly guarantee Austria, and especially hopes that all countries will entrust it with full power so that it can send troops to help Austria in the event of an emergency. If this news is true, then Italy regards Austria as a region of special interest. A few days ago, we heard that Franco-Italian negotiations encountered obstacles due to the issue of Austrian independence. Perhaps the point of conflict lies there. Now that the negotiations have returned to smooth progress, has the Italian side given up its previous proposal? Or has it obtained considerable satisfaction with the allocation of colonies? The inside story is, of course, not known to outsiders.

Judging from Laval's visit to Italy, the future of Franco-Italian cooperation seems very optimistic. If this matter can be accomplished, then the European situation can at least achieve a state of stability. Although the proposal for treaty revision may not be realized through peaceful means, Franco-Italian cooperation is still enough to make the countries in Central Europe that advocate treaty revision lose powerful leadership. Furthermore, since Austria is guaranteed by the surrounding countries, Germany's ambition to annex Austria will be even more difficult to realize. Therefore, regardless of whether Germany has the possibility of participating in the guarantee, it will not be affected in fact by its refusal to participate. Therefore, it is also not impossible to say that the cooperation between France and Italy has the same effect as the cooperation between France and Russia. In a nutshell, the purpose of the Franco-Italian rapprochement is twofold: to prevent Germany from developing to the northeast and to prevent Germany from developing to the southeast. In essence, both are intended to maintain the status quo in Europe in order to achieve temporary stability.

Roosevelt's Message to Congress Seeks Stability for the People

Recognizes that the International Situation is Deteriorating Daily

Hopes that Steady Leaders Will Turn the Tide

Strives to Avoid Being Drawn into the Whirlpool of World War

(Washington) President Roosevelt personally read his executive message to a joint session of the Senate and House of Representatives at 12:30 this afternoon, declaring that for the sake of the peace of mind of the American people, he would propose a broad plan to achieve the following: (1) Use natural resources to seek security for the lives of all the people in the country. (2) Guarantee the stability of life. (3) Guarantee the safety of respectable families. The President further stated that we have been entrusted by the people with a clear mandate. Americans must eliminate the concept of private forces manipulating public and private enterprises to seek wealth. To accomplish the above goals, we do not want to destroy desire, nor do we want to divide wealth equally. We still believe that some people should receive more rewards because of their great talents. The President continued that the desire of individuals to seek appropriate security, reasonable leisure, and a respectable life is better than the ambition to seek wealth and power. The President suggested that, within the scope of the government's economic capacity, the various public works projects should be merged into a larger-scale plan, and the federal government would no longer bear the burden of relief efforts. The President recalled the achievements of the recovery in 1934, saying that farmers had gained real benefits, and that industry and commerce were thriving, which was gratifying. The President then

Discussed International Relations

Stated that he could not honestly say that the situation outside the borders had improved. The old enemies and ambitions of the past have resurfaced in the international arena. Some countries are competing for armaments and power with fierce faces. He deeply hoped that calm and steady leaders could use their great power to turn the tide, and hoped for a steady international leader who would ultimately offer a new and practical representative government to the world. After the President's message, he dismissed the notion that the United States would be drawn into the vortex of war, and refuted the fallacy that international cooperation could not reduce or limit armaments. The President stated that maintaining international peace is a matter of deep concern to us, and there is no selfishness. We have repeatedly made concrete expressions in preventing war, so there is no reason to speculate that the United States has any ambition in its relationship with any country other than peace, etc. (National Telegram, 4th)

Support from All Parties

(Washington) President Roosevelt's personal reading of his message to a joint session of the Senate and House of Representatives at 12:30 this afternoon received unanimous support from the Democratic and Republican parties. Senate Democratic Leader Robinson stated that this message was one of the most important messages in American history, and predicted that members of both parties would work together to realize the President's intentions. Robinson continued that while there may be disagreements on the details, he believed that Congress would unanimously express satisfaction with the President's plan and purpose. Republican leaders were not as enthusiastic in their attitude, but also fully supported the President's plan and expressed full cooperation in its realization. Senate Republican Leader McNary called it a message with far-reaching vision. Republican senators also unanimously expressed their approval. House Republican Leader Snell did not want to criticize the President's message, but believed that the President's declaration could be seen as an indication of the government's shift to the right. Some observers paid particular attention to President Roosevelt's views on foreign policy, and all believed that the President's declaration would ease the situation and avoid the shipbuilding competition between Britain, the United States, and Japan after Japan abandoned the Washington Naval Treaty. (National Telegram, 4th)

Work Relief Reduces Unemployment

(Washington) The main points of President Roosevelt's address to Congress this afternoon were unemployment relief. President Roosevelt plans to revise the entire federal relief plan, advocating work relief and launching large-scale public works to abolish the method of alms. President Roosevelt pointed out that this could create a new order to guarantee social security. President Roosevelt declared that the government would adopt a plan within the scope of the government's sound credit, and said that this work included a wide range of projects. The clearing of slums, the construction of rural housing, universal electrification, the promotion of forests, the prevention of soil erosion, the opening of wasteland, the improvement of road administration, the construction of highways, and many other undertakings that the country cannot ignore, which private capital cannot handle, will be carried out in turn. This major plan is expected to absorb 3.5 million unemployed people. He has seen signs of the restoration of the spirit of credit, but he wants to warn speculators and partisan politicians not to obstruct our progress.

Almsgiving Destroys Inherent Virtues

President Roosevelt then recounted the previous temporary emergency relief legislation, saying that the number of unemployed people remains very large. The facts show that providing relief through almsgiving is a narcotic, which only destroys the spirit of people and destroys the inherent virtues of America. (Reuters Telegram, 4th)

Accumulating Wealth Should Be Repelled

In addition, President Roosevelt declared that he would read the budget message on Monday. This budget would not exceed the limit of the funds available to the government. The President would also immediately propose to Congress bills on unemployment and old-age insurance, maternal and child relief, etc. In addition, the President would also submit to Congress for consultation matters such as the federal government's strengthening of control over the transportation industry, the reform of the recovery plan, the reform of the judicial system and the veterans' association system, the restriction of the abuse of ownership, and the continued control of agriculture. The message concluded by saying that (what we call individual interests is the right of individuals to properly support themselves and their families. As for the concept of accumulating wealth, all Americans should reject it, because the result of accumulating wealth is that individuals can use excessive profits to operate their private businesses, and public affairs will inevitably suffer as a result). (Havas Telegram, 4th)

Foreign Policy Emphasizes Good Neighborliness

Referring to foreign policy, he said that he hoped that politicians from all countries would lay the foundation for the international political situation with a spirit of calm and construction, so that all countries would have the necessary time to create a new type of representative government throughout the world, so that the privileged classes could be reduced, and the welfare of the general public could be increased day by day. The President's message further stated that (currently, no country, even if it does not aspire to peace, is likely to have a conflict with our United States. There is a fallacious theory that excessive armaments cannot be reduced and limited by international agreements, and therefore the people are at risk of increasing the burden of armaments. However, the people of most countries will surely find ways to overcome the consequences of this fallacious theory. This is undoubtedly the case). (Havas Telegram, 4th)

White House Meeting to Draft New Procedures for Relief Work

Salaries of Government Officials to Be Reduced for Six Months

(Washington) President Roosevelt and seven senators and six congressmen met in the President's study today for three hours to draft new procedures for government relief work so that they could be implemented immediately. The estimated urgent need is $880 million, part of which may be taken from existing unspent relief funds. It is said that temporary relief work will be reduced as soon as possible, and the remaining relief funds will be transferred to the new procedures. The social procedures mentioned by President Roosevelt in his message to Congress yesterday will be carried out quickly. According to reliable sources, President Roosevelt has asked Congress to allocate $4 billion to launch large-scale public works so that 3.5 million people can have work. Those who attended the meeting at the President's office were Harrison, President of the New York Federal Reserve Bank, Vice President of the United States, Caleb, Senate Democratic Leader, Robinson, Senator Pittman, and Speaker of the House, Barnes, etc. (Reuters Telegram, 5th)

(Washington) According to the announcement here today, President Roosevelt is continuing to reduce the salaries of federal officials by 5% for a period of six months. The general public in political circles had hoped that full salaries could be restored after the New Year, but now they are disappointed and must wait for another six months. (Reuters Telegram, 4th)

An Uninvited Guest Suddenly Appears Before Roosevelt

Veteran Demanding Stipends is Arrested

(Washington) The crowd's cheers welcoming the President resounded through the clouds. However, when the President entered Congress, a veteran repeatedly shouted (We want stipends!), which led to his temporary detention by the police. (National Telegram, 4th)

(Washington) When President Roosevelt went to Congress this afternoon to read his message, an unidentified person approached the President, only a few meters away, and was arrested by the police. It is generally believed that the person was a communist and intended to insult the President. (Havas Telegram, 4th)

British Malaya Cracks Down on Espionage Activities

Singapore Revises Port Regulations

Foreign Soldiers Forbidden from Landing

Singapore According to new regulations published here today, soldiers or aviators from foreign warships or transport ships are not allowed to land in Singapore's ports without the permission of the government. Any ship carrying more than 100 soldiers is subject to these new regulations, except for officers who are on official visits. (Reuters Telegram, 5th)

Mussolini and Laval Meet in Venice

Three Protocols Drafted, Ready for Signing

Philippine Colonial Issue Still Under Discussion

Rome French Foreign Minister Laval arrived here at 7 pm last night. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, state officials, the French Ambassador to Italy, and French nationals gathered at the station to give him a warm welcome. This is Laval's first official return visit to Rome since 1916. After exiting the station, Laval went with Mussolini to the French Embassy, ​​and then to his hotel. It is said that Laval will have his first important meeting with Mussolini at the Venice Palace this morning. Three types of official documents have now been drafted, which are expected to be signed within days. The first is a joint declaration between France and Italy on the independence of Austria, the second is a non-interference protocol, which will be signed by Italy, Austria, Czechoslovakia, Yugoslavia, and Hungary, and the third is an agreement between France and Italy on African colonies. Regarding the understanding on colonies, Laval did not bring any experts with him on this trip, indicating that there is still important work to be done. It is said that Italy is completely dissatisfied with the territorial and railway concessions made by France and hopes that France can be more generous. (Reuters Telegram, 5th)

Communiqué Issued

Rome French Foreign Minister Laval met with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini at the Venice Palace this morning. When arriving at the palace, he received a fascist salute. Upon entering the conference room, the Italian Prime Minister reached out to welcome him. According to the authorities, the talks between the French Foreign Minister and the Italian Prime Minister this morning lasted for two hours. The French Ambassador to Rome and the Italian Deputy Foreign Minister were present. It was also said that a First Secretary of the French Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Deputy Director of African Affairs went to the Zhiji Palace to discuss current issues.

Audience with the Italian King

After the talks, Laval had an audience with the Italian King and did not leave the palace until lunchtime. Soldiers and police lined the streets along Laval's route. This morning, the Chargé d'Affaires of Abyssinia also had an audience with the Italian King. It is said that Italy is eager to make its peaceful intentions clear to the Abyssinian people, as the tense situation between the two countries could obstruct the friendly agreement between France and Italy. (Reuters Telegram, 5th)

Rome The agreement between France and Italy is still being prepared. It is generally believed that it cannot be finalized before Sunday evening. After having dinner at the Embassy last night, French Foreign Minister Laval went to work at the Hotel Excelsior and did not go to bed until late at night. At 9:30 this morning, Laval went to the Venice Palace to meet with Prime Minister Mussolini, and they discussed the various diplomatic issues in Europe for about two hours. However, the nature of this talk was, of course, general and will need to be supplemented by more precise talks later. On the other hand, experts from France and Italy will also study in detail solutions to various issues related to the African colonies. After Laval and the Prime Minister finished talking, they went to pay their respects to King Emmanuel III. The King invited him for a light meal. The Prime Minister is scheduled to host a banquet at the Venice Palace tonight to welcome Laval. (Havas Telegram, 5th)

Conclusion of Pact Guaranteeing Peace in Central Europe is Hopeful

(Rome) The first important meeting between Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and French Foreign Minister Laval this morning has been going smoothly. There is great hope for the conclusion of a pact to guarantee peace in Europe. Hungary's reserved attitude towards the Austrian issue has made it necessary to establish a temporary solution to maintain Hungary's rights. After Hungary is satisfied with this, the future of the European situation has become optimistic. The Italian and French governments now firmly agree that Austrian independence must be maintained. The pact to protect Austrian independence will invite Germany, Yugoslavia, Czechoslovakia, and Hungary to participate. Hungary has expressed conditional support. As for Hungary's conditions, it will still retain its consistent policy of revising the Treaty of Saint-Germain, but will allow its actions not to go beyond the scope of the League of Nations Covenant. Therefore, it will never use war or any violence as a tool to achieve its national aspirations. In addition, Mussolini and Laval also agreed to delineate the borders of Libya and the new status of Italians in Tunisia. These two issues have long been a source of trouble between the two countries. The first meeting this morning began to disperse at 11:30. French Foreign Minister Laval then paid his respects to the Italian King and did not retire for about half an hour. (National Telegram, 5th)

France Concedes Philippine Colonial Issue, Italy Not Satisfied

(Paris) Reliable news: The Rome Agreement stipulates that the French government will cede 500,000 square miles of its Sahara territory to Italy. The Sahara is inhabited by more than 200,000 Tebou people. It is also said that Italy is demanding land up to Lake Chad, but the French government wants to retain a 500-mile-wide corridor area. (National Telegram, 5th)

Britain Holds High Hopes

(London) The British government fully agrees with the goals of the negotiations now underway between Italy and France in Rome. A communiqué was recently issued stating that the British government has instructed Sir Drummond, the British Ambassador to Italy, to express to Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and French Foreign Minister Laval in the personal name of Foreign Secretary Simon his fervent hope that the current negotiations will be successful. (Havas Telegram, 5th)

Austria Optimistic

Vienna Foreign Minister Berger recently issued a statement to the press expressing optimism about the results of French Foreign Minister Laval's trip to Rome to hold talks with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. He said that Chancellor Schuschnigg and he were particularly pleased with the Franco-Italian negotiations. The non-interference pact being negotiated by France and Italy in Rome stipulates that the signatory countries have the obligation not to interfere in the internal affairs of other signatory countries, but he hopes to go further and stipulate that it is forbidden to encourage or even tolerate any actions that endanger other signatory countries in any way. Berger also said that the Austrian government has successfully made Austria and Western European countries an important partnership. The plan for the Austrian Chancellor and Foreign Minister to visit Britain and France should further clarify the situation. (Havas Telegram, 5th)

Poland Suspicious

The Warsaw government's newspapers seemed quite surprised to hear of French Foreign Minister Laval's trip to Rome. They mostly expressed doubts about the outcome of Laval's trip. However, the right-wing anti-government newspapers strongly affirmed the importance of the rapprochement between France and Italy and said that the Polish government had not tried to eliminate the estrangement between France and Poland, which was inappropriate. (Havas Telegram, 4th)

Unease in Hungary

The visit of French Foreign Minister Laval to Rome appears to have caused considerable anxiety and unease in Hungary. The Hungarian Telegraphic Agency commented on the matter, stating that the Franco-Italian negotiations would not address the issue of a territorial guarantee pact. This is because once a territorial guarantee pact is established, modifying treaties through peaceful means would become impossible. Therefore, regardless of the outcome of the Rome talks, it should not affect the principles of the Hungarian government. (Havas dispatch, 5th)

Budapest is paying close attention to the talks between French Foreign Minister Laval and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, as the Rome agreement has strengthened Italo-Hungarian relations. Regarding the revision of treaties, semi-official sources say Mussolini will maintain his original intention of safeguarding Hungarian interests, recognizing Hungarian demands as the only way to maintain stability in the Danube region. Newspapers report that Hungary's lifeline is closely tied to Italy and Germany, with political and economic relations with Germany being particularly essential. Hungary cannot accept French media claims that Germany is a common enemy of France, Italy, and Hungary. In reality, Hungary hopes for cooperation between Germany and Italy. (National Telegram, 4th)

Predictions for the European and American Political Situation in 1935

May: Overthrow of the French Republic, Restoration of the Monarchy. Saar Plebiscite Expected to Pass Peacefully. A Major European Statesman Assassinated Within Two Months. Osaka Mainichi Shimbun carries a special dispatch from Paris. The saying "(Crisis of 1935-1936)" is not only popular in Japan, but also causes great concern in Europe. As this year is 1935, the changes that will occur are attracting much social attention. Someone visited three famous female fortune tellers in Paris: Marno-Dai, Viday, and Cloudet. These three are incredibly knowledgeable and have a proven track record of accurately predicting future political, economic, diplomatic, medical, and other events. The following is a summary of their predictions: (France will have minor issues with its northern neighbors. The economic situation in February will be quite good. Commercial prosperity in March and April will restore the advantage of five or six years ago. The stock market will rise, and unemployment will decrease. This year will be peaceful and without war. The Saar plebiscite will also pass uneventfully, although no one will be satisfied. However, within the next two months, a major foreign statesman will be assassinated. The perpetrator will be a Polish person, an Italian, or a lilac-colored student. Mussolini is safe from harm. After the French general election in May, there will be a change in the national structure, overthrowing the republic. Seven years later, the monarchy will be restored. The United States is expected to have sound currency this year. A cure for cancer and tuberculosis may be completed this year. There will be major incidents at sea and in the air. A major earthquake is also unavoidable. By 1937, there will be a severe epidemic.)

Japan Retains Control of Mandated Islands, U.S. Temporarily Does Not Interfere

But Declares Right to Comment

(Washington) Official sources here stated today that the United States does not wish to immediately interfere with Japan's continued mandate over the former German islands in the Pacific. However, officials firmly asserted that, although the United States is not a member of the League of Nations, it has the right to comment on this matter and may exercise its right to resolve the issue at any time. The U.S. Navy Department is quite concerned about reports from Geneva regarding new facilities built by Japan on the mandated islands. These islands are located along routes that U.S. merchant ships must take between the American coast to the east and the Philippines. (National Telegram, 4th)

(London) The League of Nations Mandates Commission released a report in Geneva yesterday, stating that Japan's construction of seaports on the mandated islands in the Pacific is costing a great deal, which is disproportionate to the commercial relations of those islands. France's Reply to U.S. Note Explains Naval Stance

Hopes to Conclude New Treaty to Replace Old One (Washington) French Ambassador to the United States, De Laboulaye, sent a note to the U.S. government this evening, explaining the French government's views on naval issues. The note stated that France hopes that all naval powers, other than the five nations of Great Britain, the United States, Japan, France, and Italy, will also participate in signing a new treaty to replace the Washington Naval Treaty. The note also stated that when the French government requested parliamentary approval to ratify the Washington Naval Treaty, Parliament indicated that the treaty should not be extended after it expires in 1936. When the French government ratified the treaty, it also notified the United States that the 5:5:3 ratio stipulated in the treaty was not suitable for the situation of each country and could only be applied to armored ships and aircraft carriers, but not to other types of warships. The final paragraph of the note stated that the navies of countries outside the signatories of the Washington Treaty should also be considered, because when the Washington Naval Treaty was signed, their navies were not significant, but now the situation is very different. (Referring to the German navy) (Havas dispatch, 4th)

Promote the Japan-Manchukuo Economic Group

Expand Intelligence and Special Agencies

(Changchun) General Minami, Commander of the Kwantung Army, and Major General Itagaki, Deputy Chief of Staff, have recently agreed on a fundamental policy toward Manchuria. The main points are divided into two types: (1) The Japan-Manchukuo Economic Group. (A) Establish the economic value of Dalian. (B) Reorganization of the South Manchuria Railway (SMR). The SMR Company is recognized as a financial component of the Japan-Manchukuo economic group, so its reorganization should not disperse its financial resources. However, it must be made a purely national policy company. Based on Japan's policy of governing Manchukuo, first merge the SMR with the railways of eastern provinces to form a large railway company. (2) Expansion of intelligence agencies. With the international crisis imminent, the Kwantung Army and the intelligence and special agencies within the Manchukuo organization must be expanded and controlled. It is planned to organize a joint Japan-Manchukuo central intelligence and propaganda control agency in Changchun. (3) Reorganization of the Kwantung Army internally. It is planned to replace most of the personnel in March of this year, eliminate elements from different factions, and reorganize the ranks. (Hualian dispatch, 5th)

British Lord Privy Seal Eden's Speech on the International Situation

This Year Is the Most Important Year

Praises the League of Nations for Handling Matters Appropriately

European War Temporarily Avoided

(London) Lord Privy Seal Eden spoke last night in Newcastle on the international situation, saying that there has been much talk of the danger of war recently, but he does not believe that war will break out in the near future. If war were to break out, it would not only harm the conquered, but the victors would also suffer. Eden acknowledged that 1934 was an eventful year, but in the final weeks, the international situation showed definite and even surprising progress, largely due to the League of Nations Council's appropriate handling of dangerous issues such as the Saar plebiscite and the South Hungarian dispute. The Council meetings convened specifically for these two issues were among the most important events in the history of the League of Nations. The first issue concerned maintaining order during the plebiscite period. The British government's suggestion to send troops to join the League of Nations international force stationed in the Saar resolved the issue smoothly. The second issue was even more difficult. The unfortunate assassination of King Alexander of Yugoslavia in Marseille strained relations between Yugoslavia and Hungary, threatening the maintenance of peace. Therefore, the special responsibility of advocating a fair attitude fell on the shoulders of the British government representative. The League of Nations Council dared to say that within a week, it had found a way to deal with two issues that could greatly damage good relations between European countries, and a satisfactory final outcome was expected. Eden continued that he believed that the organization of an international air force to serve as the world's police force would likely be realized in the future, but the time was not yet ripe. Such a force cannot be realized in an armed world and will only be effective after the world disarms. However, we are still far from this period. He strongly agreed with General Smuts' statement that the League of Nations should not be regarded as a military organization. It would be a mistake to try to create such an organization. Eden concluded by discussing the future of 1935, saying that we are now standing at the threshold of the most important year in post-war history, but we must not be deterministic or self-deprecating. 1935 will prove whether we can make the League of Nations effective. As for him personally, he is optimistic. (Reuters dispatch, 5th)

Saar Plebiscite Approaching

Residents Gradually Showing Signs of Unease

Opposing German Factions Hold Separate Gatherings Across the River

Authorities Make Careful Arrangements to Maintain Order During the Plebiscite

Saarbrücken, Saar As the date of the Saar plebiscite approaches, residents throughout the region are gradually showing signs of unease. The tranquility of the past few days is maintained by the wisdom and courage of the international police force. No one dares to predict that voters will advocate for belonging to France, so the Socialist Party and the Communist Party are both afraid for their own positions, doing everything in their power to maintain the status quo and prevent the Saar from returning to Germany. Some Catholics also support this movement because they fear that Hitlerism will destroy the Catholic organization. Tomorrow, opposing parties will hold separate public gatherings, so the police and gendarmes have prepared high-speed cars and open-top vehicles to patrol the city. To prevent conflicts, the authorities have ordered party members to gather across the river at different times and have prohibited wearing uniforms and carrying flags. The results of the vote on the 13th will not be known until two days later. The authorities will implement the most thorough plan to ensure the secrecy of the vote. An outsider will be stationed at each polling place to oversee the process. Voters will seal the ballot they cast and hand it to the supervisor, who will seal it again before putting it into the ballot box. In total, there are 540,000 votes. General speculation focuses on the number of votes to maintain the status quo. Non-optimistic members of the Nazi Party say it could reach 200,000 votes, while enthusiastic supporters of Hitler estimate that this type of vote will not exceed 50,000. The police authorities have ordered the troops to act with caution and be on high alert, but should try to avoid publicity. (Reuters dispatch, 5th)

Neustadt Neustadt A Reuters reporter visited Saar Commissioner Buckel, who was sent by Hitler. Judging from his remarks, Germany has made various preparations to take over the Saar. Buckel said that anyone who opposes Germany and has lived in the Saar for less than three years will be charged with treason if they remain in the Saar after it returns to Germany. Buckel also firmly stated that the German government sincerely wishes to not investigate the past. At the same time, according to a Reuters dispatch from Saarbrücken, the Saar Governing Commission has asked Prince Hubertus, a well-known anti-Nazi, to leave the country within 48 hours because his passport and other documents do not comply with regulations. Also, according to a dispatch from Paris, the French Minister of the Interior has instructed county magistrates and mayors across the country to prepare to receive Saar immigrants, to prevent a majority of voters advocating for belonging to Germany in the plebiscite on January 13. Judging from the current situation, the outcome of the plebiscite will be unfavorable to France. Paris now believes that if the Saar returns to Germany, about 30,000 residents of the region will wish to immigrate to France. (Reuters dispatch, 5th)

Saarbrücken The Saar Regional Plebiscite Commission will announce the rules for the Saar Regional Plebiscite on January 13 tomorrow, and will also explain the support for maintaining the status quo and continuing the League of Nations' administration in light of the voting results. According to the Treaty of Versailles, the plebiscite can choose from (1) merger with Germany, (2) merger with France, and (3) maintaining the status quo. After the League of Nations Council meeting in December, it was decided that if the majority supports maintaining the status quo, the situation can change in the future, and the people of the Saar can still hold another plebiscite to determine their sovereignty. This is still not in violation of the Treaty of Versailles. This explanation will be made public for the first time in tomorrow's announcement. (Havas dispatch, 4th)

Inside Story of the Major Bribery Scandal in Japan (Japan News)

Political Parties Greatly Influenced

Financial Circles Feel Immense Difficulty

In recent years in Japan, alongside the prevalence of extraordinary times, cases of bribery and corruption have emerged one after another. Among the major cases, the Ministry of Finance incident is the most prominent. This case involves Finance Vice-Minister Hideo Kuroda, Banking Bureau Director Teiji Okubo, and implicates former Railway President Chuzo Mitsuchi, Commerce and Industry Minister Baron Hisamankichi Nakajima, and numerous other influential figures in banking and business circles. The Saito Cabinet was even attacked by the Diet because of this, and with cabinet members being implicated in dishonorable matters, the cabinet consequently collapsed.

Tracing back to the occurrence of this incident, it originated from the Bank of Taiwan extending loans to Suzuki & Co. Since the end of the World War, the company had been affected by the unfavorable economic situation, making it difficult to continue operations. The loans it borrowed from the Bank of Taiwan became impossible to repay. At that time, the Bank of Taiwan also engaged in excessively lenient lending, resulting in 350 million in loans that could not be recovered as scheduled. Consequently, except for its branches on Taiwan Island and overseas that were barely maintained, the bank temporarily suspended operations in Japan. Subsequently, the Bank of Japan stepped in to maintain and rescue it, providing accommodation of over 100 million in cash, allowing it to reopen. The stocks of various businesses operated by Suzuki & Co., held by the Bank of Taiwan, mostly entered the Bank of Japan's treasury and were managed by the Bank of Japan. Among them was the stock of Teikoku Rayon Co., Ltd. After 1932, Japan's light industry developed upward, exports of cotton cloth gradually increased, and rayon fabrics became even more prosperous. Teikoku Rayon benefited equally, and its business suddenly flourished. Not only did it have no inventory, but its output for two or three months was already fully booked. As a result, the company's stock gradually soared, reaching more than twice the par value.

At that time, Bank of Taiwan President Shigeru Shimada, seeing the great profit at hand, was unwilling to give it up. He secretly conspired with Teikoku Rayon President Fukuko Takagi, Director Akira Okazaki, and Auditor Yoshinari Kawai to discuss how to bypass the Ministry of Finance and deceive the Bank of Japan, preparing funds to take 100,000 shares of Teikoku Rayon stock from the bank and sell them in Tokyo and Osaka, to divide the profits. At that time, it was also agreed to increase the company's dividend distribution for the second half of last year by 3 percent. The company's stock then soared even higher, approaching a market price of 200 yen per share, while the selling price was only 125 yen per share. The Bank of Taiwan's losses from this were estimated to be over 12 million yen.

After Shimada and others finalized their plan, they proceeded separately to take out the stock and sell it. Furthermore, since the stock involved numbered about several hundred thousand shares, and the funds involved were over ten million, the turnover became a problem. For those who mediated, they could not be rewarded with cash. Therefore, they proposed 1,300 shares of Teikoku Rayon stock to reward those involved. According to reports, former Vice-Minister of Finance Hideo Kuroda received 400 shares (market value slightly over 60,000 yen), former Railway President Chuzo Mitsuchi 300 shares (approximately 45,000 yen), former Commerce and Industry Minister Hisamankichi Nakajima 200 shares (valued at 30,000 yen), and former Banking Bureau Director Teiji Okubo 100 shares (valued at 15,000 yen). Such distribution amounted to only 2 percent of the huge profit of over 10 million yen. Both Chuzo Mitsuchi and Hisamankichi Nakajima were famous figures of their time and key figures in the Seiyukai political party, while Kuroda was also a top choice in the Ministry of Finance. It is unexpected that they would all be suspected of bribery today, which is quite surprising to the world. However, Mitsuchi still does not admit to accepting bribes and cites facts, stating that he absolutely did not accept the stock or exchange it for cash, and even points out the errors in the dates cited by the Tokyo District Court, to clarify that he has no involvement. At the same time, the Ministry of Finance has also publicly stated that those implicated in the Ministry will definitely not accept bribes, and that the truth will come to light in the future. This has further raised a major issue, namely, confessions obtained through torture during preliminary hearings, forcing the defendants to fabricate facts. Extrapolating to this point, the sanctity of judicial power and the trampling of humanity have become a major issue. In short, this matter has a great bearing on Japan's political future. If the court's investigation is confirmed, the political world will suffer unprecedented infamy. If Mitsuchi and others' denials prove to be correct, then the spirit of the judiciary will also be swept away. Which of the two is true remains to be proven by future facts. (December 28, Tokyo)

Elements of the Minbian Mutiny Arrested

Provincial Party Headquarters Promulgates Measures for Communist Surrender

Fuzhou Correspondence: Recently, the authorities have been paying close attention to the actions of those involved in last year's Minbian Mutiny. Huang Wan was arrested in Fuzhou, and Zhang Shengcai was arrested in Xiamen. Huang had served as a member of the Economic Committee of the Provisional People's Government. After the failure, he fled to Hong Kong and recently sneaked back to Fuzhou. The special task force of the Provincial Party Headquarters discovered this and arrested him, detaining him at the Provincial Party Headquarters. Zhang had served as the chairman of the Xiamen Cultural Movement Grand Alliance and announced his separation from the Kuomintang. He was recently arrested by the Xiamen Public Security Bureau and sent to the province, detained at the Military Law Section of the Security Office. However, both Huang and Zhang have considerable status in society, so many people from various circles are running around trying to rescue them. It is reported that the authorities have telegraphed the Central Government, requesting instructions on how to handle the matter. In addition, in Putian and Lianjiang, several Communist Party offenders have also been arrested recently and sent to the Security Office for interrogation. Regarding the surrender of Communists, since the establishment of the Communist Party Surrender Review Committee, the Commissioner's Office of the Provincial Party Headquarters has formulated nine articles of measures for accepting the surrender of Communists. From now on, all surrenders of Communists in this province should be applied for directly to the office in accordance with the law. All Communist Party surrender cases accepted by various political, military, and police agencies, regardless of whether they have been reviewed, should also have the original files transferred to the office for review by the Review Committee or for filing. The contents of the measures are explored and recorded below. Article 1: This office formulates these measures in accordance with the provisions of Article 5 of the Communist Party Surrender Law to accept Communist Party surrender cases. Article 2: Communists may apply to this office for surrender in accordance with the Communist Party Surrender Law. Article 3: When surrendering, the surrendering person should personally write an application, detailing the following items separately: (1) Name, (2) Age, (3) Native place, (4) Family address and personal address, (5) Origin, (6) Date of joining the Communist Party, (7) Place of joining the Communist Party, (8) Introducer to the Communist Party, (9) Section of affiliation after joining, (10) Work undertaken after joining (detailed by date), (11) Comrades who have had contact after joining, their addresses, and positions, (12) Reasons for surrender, (13)

Page 10

(13) Evidence of sincere surrender, (14) Tendencies after surrender and willingness to undertake any work. If the aforementioned items cannot be written by oneself, a person may be commissioned to write on their behalf. The surrendering person should affix their fingerprint and the writing agent should sign and affix their seal. Article 4: The aforementioned surrender application should be submitted to this office along with three recent 4-inch half-length photos of the surrendering person for review by the Communist Party Surrender Case Review Committee. The aforementioned Review Committee shall be organized by one representative each from the Fujian Provincial Government, the High Court, the Security Office, the Fuzhou Garrison Headquarters, the Military Police Regiment, the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, and this office, with the representative of this office serving as a standing committee member. Article 5: Upon receiving the aforementioned surrender application, the Review Committee shall immediately dispatch personnel or recommend personnel to investigate, and invite the surrendering person to fill out a registration form and a guarantee. The aforementioned guarantee must be signed and sealed by three party members of this party and three citizens of this province with legitimate occupations. Article 6: After the Review Committee deliberates and decides on the surrender case, it shall send the case along with its review opinions to the Security Office or the competent court for adjudication. For serious cases or cases where the surrender is not sincere, the surrendering person may be sent along with the case. Article 7: The competent court authorities shall notify the Review Committee after handling the surrender case so that it can be reported to the Central Government. Article 8: Matters not stipulated in these measures shall be handled in accordance with the Communist Party Surrender Law and its related criminal laws. Article 9: These measures shall be implemented after being decided by this office and reported to the Central Executive Committee for filing. (December 29)

Second Phase of Rural Cooperative Work Completed in Henan Province

Trial Implementation in Twenty-Seven Counties, Seven Hundred Societies Established

Loans Issued Nearly 400,000 Yuan

Kaifeng Correspondence: The rural cooperative movement in Henan Province, since the establishment of the committee in April last year, has completed the second phase of work by the end of last year. Twenty-seven counties have been selected for trial implementation, and more than 700 cooperative societies have been established, with loans issued reaching 400,000 yuan. The details are recorded as follows: Zhang Jingyu and Wu Jing were commissioned by the Nanchang Headquarters as members of the Henan Rural Cooperative Committee in the winter of the 22nd year of the Republic (1933-1934), and Zhang was appointed as chairman and Wu as general manager. They actively prepared and formally established the cooperative committee in April of the 23rd year of the Republic (1934-1935), assigning more than 60 people trained in Jiangxi, including Fan Zhi, to serve as instructors. Initially, only Kaifeng, Zhengzhou, Shangqiu, Anyang, Huixian, Xinxiang, Luoyang, Shaanzhou, Saishan, Xuchang, Yuxian, Nanyang, Runan, Huaiyang, and other fourteen counties were designated as trial counties. After several months of promotion, the results were quite good. Subsequently, as the committee affairs became increasingly complex, Xu Qinglan was added as a committee member and general inspector through the approval of the headquarters. By the end of the first phase of work at the end of August, the cooperative societies established in various counties had reached over 200. Since the start of the second phase of work, there has been even greater progress than before. The trial counties have successively increased to include Guangwu, Rongyang, Huaxian, Qinyang, Xiangcheng, Zhenping, Yuanyang, Xinzheng, Mixian, Lanfeng, Mengxian, and Mianchi, and other thirteen counties. The method of organizing cooperative societies begins with publicity and investigation, first teaching farmers simple cooperative knowledge, making them clearly understand the benefits of cooperation, and voluntarily forming societies, then guiding them to handle the establishment procedures and operate their businesses. Therefore, they have repeatedly received commendations from the headquarters. Currently, the 27 trial counties have established more than 700 cooperative societies, and the total amount of loans granted to various cooperative societies is nearly 400,000 yuan, most of which is supplied by the Four Provinces Farmers Bank, and there is also investment from the Tianjin China Bank. The association has also cooperated with the Agricultural College of Henan University, with the Agricultural College handing over successfully tested wheat seeds to the association for distribution to the utilization cooperative societies under its guidance for planting, in order to promote and strive for widespread adoption. Recently, a technical design committee has been organized, inviting Wang Jinwu, president of the Agricultural College of Henan University, professors Li Xianwen, Lin Shize, Xu Zhenying, and Liu Wenbin and Xu Baikui, section chiefs of the Construction Department, to serve as committee members, planning to improve the cooperative society's products, animal husbandry, and the construction of agricultural, forestry, and water conservancy projects. This year, it is planned to hold large-scale warehouses in Shaanzhou, Lingbao, Yuanyang, Luoyang, and other cotton-producing areas to handle storage, mortgage, transportation, and sales, so as to prevent farmers from being exploited by unscrupulous merchants. (3rd)

Bombing Cases in Guangzhou City During the Year-End Season

Bomb Explodes at White Cloud Hotel, East Window

One Hotel Employee Injured on the Spot

Two Threatening Letters Reported Together

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since the division of Guangdong Province for pacification, the leading bandits in various places have successively disappeared or fled overseas, while scattered small groups still lurk and commit petty crimes from time to time. As the year-end season approaches, the bold and fierce are out extorting money, and boatmen have been repeatedly threatened. Therefore, since winter, joint shipping on various river ferries has implemented self-defense. Initially, only those in the shipping industry were wary, but recently, the rampant activity has become even worse, and they are even extorting money from large hotels in the city center, where military and police are stationed. When extortion fails, they throw bombs to harass them. This is truly blatant and without any scruples. Previously, the White Cloud Hotel on Guangzhou's Changdi, a large and well-regarded hotel with seven or eight floors standing tall on the riverbank, offering both dining and lodging, had been attracting crowds of customers every day since its opening in July of this year, attracting the attention of bandits. A letter, signed by the leader He Duan of the West River Flying Dragon Hall bandit gang, was sent, stating that the brothers were suffering from a lack of food and were asking the hotel for a loan of 1,000 yuan. Mr. Lu, the manager of the hotel's dining department, considered bandit extortion to be commonplace and ignored it. More than a month later, on the 27th of this month, a second threatening letter was received, with many threatening words, roughly stating that the previous request for a loan of 1,000 yuan had not been fulfilled as scheduled and that this was a reminder, limiting them to paying the loan immediately, otherwise they would be dealt with severely. The manager also laughed it off. Unexpectedly, on that day, as the hotel's dining department was closing, customers were leaving one after another, and the staff were sweeping up. Suddenly, in guest seat No. 16 in the east corner, a cigarette pack was spotted. Hotel employee Yu Bin picked it up and examined it, seeing that there were still cigarettes inside and something heavy. Knowing that something was wrong, he quickly threw the cigarette pack out the window. The cigarette pack hit the window post and exploded with a loud bang. Iron filings flew everywhere. Everyone knew it was the sound of a bomb and rushed forward to rescue. At that time, Yu Bin had already fallen to the ground, and thick smoke filled the room. A window was destroyed. Police detectives rushed to the scene to investigate, searching nearby pedestrians, but found no suspicious figures. It was suspected that the bomb had been pre-placed by the bandits, waiting for a hotel employee to pick it up, triggering the explosion. After inspection, the police detectives determined that it was undoubtedly placed by bandits and sent the injured hotel employee Yu Bin to the Municipal Hospital for treatment. At the same time, manager Lu Yiqing also reported the bombing to the Jinghai Public Security Bureau, along with the two previous threatening letters received from the bandits, requesting a swift resolution to the case and the arrest of the culprits, in order to maintain commerce. As for the injured Yu Bin, after being sent to the hospital, the doctor bandaged the wound on his left shoulder. Fortunately, he was not seriously injured and was discharged from the hospital after pain relief to recuperate at home. (December 30)

Nanjing Zheng Society Holds Third Exhibition

The Zheng Society of Wu, founded by Wu Hufan, Peng Gongfu, Pan Boshan, Chen Ziqing, and others, focuses on the study of ancient and modern painting and calligraphy art. At the end of last year, the Wu County Association of Fellow Townsmen in Beijing held an opening ceremony and specially displayed the society's works for one day. Guests, such as Chairman Lin and key figures from various Yuan departments, praised them highly. However, many who were not invited by the association regretted not being able to see them. Therefore, it was decided to formally hold the Zheng Society's Third Painting and Calligraphy Exhibition, starting on the 5th of this month, at the Central Hotel here. It is estimated that about 400 to 500 pieces of work created by the members themselves and ancient and modern works of previous dynasties collected by the members will be displayed. Robbery and Injury at Tianmashan Mountain in Songjiang

Tianmashan, map 37, is more than 20 miles from Songjiang and is a thoroughfare. On the evening of the 3rd, robbers speaking in a Jiangbei accent, holding Browning pistols, broke into the home of villager Xu Caiyuan through the window. They threatened and prohibited the victim from making a sound, searching wantonly. Caiyuan's son, Qiuyun, resisted slightly, and the robbers fired two shots, hitting him and knocking him to the ground. The robbers fled with the loot. After checking, ten silver dollars and dozens of pieces of silk and cloth were stolen. The injured Xu Qiuyun has been sent to St. Joseph's Hospital for treatment. It is reported that he is not in life-threatening condition.

Nanhui County Magistrate Sells Calligraphy to Repair Government Office

Nanhui County Magistrate Xi Luo Yuan, after taking office for more than a year, has maintained integrity, and handled local affairs with great enthusiasm. He particularly promoted the adoption of the Gregorian calendar. Last year, seeing that the government office was dilapidated and there were no funds to repair it, he sold calligraphy for several months, renovating it as much as possible, making it look brand new. He then held a large-scale celebration on New Year's Day this year, and all shops closed for one day to show their promotion of the Gregorian calendar.

Suzhou Requests Ban on Electric Hair Perming

Electric hair perming has recently become popular in Suzhou. Modern women are rushing to it. However, electric hair perming is very dangerous. Many people have suffered head burns and injuries due to poor skills of hairdressers. Yesterday (the 5th), several women, including Li Xuezhen, jointly filed a petition with the county government, requesting that the Public Security Bureau be strictly ordered to ban electric hair perming to avoid danger.

Water Police Strictly Guard Against Lake Bandits

Since the start of winter, theft cases have occurred frequently in the four rural districts, and villagers have been unable to sleep peacefully at night. Zhou, the district chief of the Second Water Public Security District, in view of this, has strictly ordered the detachments stationed in Wujiang, Changshu, Kunshan, Pingwang, and along Taihu Lake to patrol once every three days. In case of bandit alarm, they can notify the nearby police team by telephone for assistance. Also, it is reported that Zhang Guifang, the captain of the 9th team of the district, has been suspended from duty and Yan Heling has been appointed as his replacement. Wu Gang, the captain of the special task force, has been transferred to the position of captain of the 10th team, and Xing Mo has been appointed to fill the vacancy.

Wuxi Telegram Requests Cancellation of Anhui Disaster Relief Donation

The oil mill trade association of this county telegraphed, stating that regarding the request to cancel the Anhui disaster relief donation, the Executive Yuan has issued an order to cancel it within December. However, the deadline has now passed, and the disaster relief donation organizations in various parts of Anhui are still collecting it, citing that they have not received provincial orders. We earnestly request your association to strive together to achieve complete success, it is urgently requesting this county's chamber of commerce to transfer these facts to the Executive Yuan, requesting that it quickly order the Anhui Provincial Government to cancel all kinds of grain-carrying disaster relief donations immediately, in order to maintain credibility, and to alleviate the suffering of the people of Jiangsu.

Suicide of Young Man at Taihu Hotel

Zhao Changsheng (Dingxin), a staff member of the engineering section of the Xinji Silk Factory in Tongyangqiao, outside the South Gate, was from Shanghai and was 19 years old. He was diligent in his work and deeply trusted by the factory owner. On the afternoon of the 31st of last month, Zhao suddenly asked the accounting department for leave and left the factory, going directly to the Taihu Hotel in Meiyuan, booking room No. 8, and hiring a photographer from the Meiyuan Photo Studio to take a photo. He then went out for sightseeing, returning to the inn at around 6:00 p.m. for dinner before going to bed. Unexpectedly, by 10:00 a.m. on New Year's Day, Zhao had not yet gotten up. Tea server Yu Aqi called out to him, but there was no response. He entered through the side door and suddenly saw Zhao's face pale, moaning on the bed. Knowing that he had taken poison, he immediately reported to the accounting department and urgently invited doctors such as Zhu Chaoliang from the Tongren Hospital to rush to his rescue. It was determined that he had taken sleeping pills. An operation was immediately performed, and he was taken back to the hospital for treatment. However, due to the severe poisoning, he died at 7:30 p.m. Several suicide notes were found, addressed to relatives and friends. His mother has now come to Wuxi to collect the body. It is reported that the reason for his suicide was a broken heart.

Missing Policeman's Corpse Found

Hu Wenxiu, a first-grade policeman from the Second Police Station of the First Public Security Bureau, suddenly disappeared around 3:00 AM on December 18th of last year. At the same time, both the police station and Hu's family received his suicide note, stating that he could not maintain his livelihood due to economic pressure and had committed suicide by drowning in Taihu Lake. Although searches were conducted everywhere at the time, no trace was found. Yesterday morning, an unidentified male corpse was suddenly discovered in Yaojiawan, Map 268 of District 3. The map leader, Hu Guanbao, immediately reported it to the local sub-court for examination. A prosecutor, accompanied by clerks, went to examine the body and confirmed that the death was due to drowning after injury. Later, someone noticed that the corpse resembled Hu and immediately notified Hu's wife, Wang, to identify it.

Zhenjiang Collecting Spring Business Tax

The Zhenyang Business Tax Bureau announced that it was time to collect the spring business tax for the 24th year of the Republic, and yesterday issued a notice informing businesses to pay taxes on time. With the approval of the Provincial Finance Department, collection will begin on the first day of the first month of each quarter and continue until the end of the following month. Those who fail to pay on time will be penalized with a late payment fee of one-tenth of the tax amount. For delays exceeding one month, the penalty will be two-tenths, and for delays exceeding two months, business operations will be suspended.

Major Fire in Hangzhou at Night, Three Deaths

In Hangzhou, a fire broke out at the Su Yi shop of Guo Xianglin on Shiban Lane, Dongjielu, at 2:30 AM this morning (the 5th), due to carelessness in cooking a late-night snack. It was late at night, and Guo's family was all asleep. By the time the fire became intense, they were finally alerted and scrambled to escape. By the time the fire brigade arrived, the fire had already spread to the left and right. After strenuous efforts to extinguish it, it was finally put out after an hour and a half. Nineteen houses were burned down, with losses exceeding 20,000 yuan. When the fire started, Guo's wife, Yu, 34 years old, his son, Songquan, 12 years old, and his daughter, Shunjin, 10 years old, were unable to escape and perished in the flames. Guo himself suffered severe burns to his head, his hair was burned off, his face was charred, and his legs were injured. He is currently being treated in the hospital.

Financial and Military Reduction Bonds Drawn Yesterday for Redemption

Three bonds drawn, totaling 660,000 Silver Dollars

Financial 15, Military Reduction begins payment at the end of the month

The 12th drawing of the Republic of China's 20th Year Financial Short-Term Bonds and the 18th drawing of the Republic of China's 18th Year Military Reduction Bonds for repayment of principal were held at 10:00 AM yesterday in the conference hall of the Hong Kong Road Bankers' Association. More than 30 representatives from various sectors attended. The drawing was presided over by Jiang Lufu, the Director of the Public Debt Department. A total of three bonds were drawn, with a total repayment of 660,000 silver dollars. All winning bonds will be paid by the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications in various locations, starting on the 15th of this month for the Financial Bonds and on the 31st of this month for the Military Reduction Bonds. Details are listed as follows:

List of Attendees

Attendees included Jiang Lufu, Director of the Public Debt Department; Wang Qichang from the Auditing Department as supervisor; Chen Zhaqing from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce; Fan Jietang from the National Debt Fund Management Committee; Lin Kanghou from the Shanghai Bankers' Association; Chen Shengwu from the Shanghai Money Dealers' Association; Jin Jingyuan from the Central Bank as lottery drawer; Zhu Qizhen from the Bank of China; Mao Shijian from the Bank of Communications; He Xiaoyuan, Zong Boxuan, and Liang Yaozong as managers; You Dundi, Ji Juncai, and Fang Jingzhong as registrars; Wang Huifen, Dong Qizong, Ling Xun, and Huang Meizhao as document clerks; Gong Baozhen, Zheng Yijian, Chen Jian, and Xu Bangzheng as receptionists; Luo Huizong from the Hankou Chamber of Commerce; Dong Xuntian from the Beiping Chamber of Commerce; Hua Shihao from the Guohua Bank; Pan Yonghe from the Zhejiang Industrial Bank; and more than 30 others.

Chairman's Report

After the usual formalities, Chairman Jiang Lufu reported, briefly stating: "Today is the drawing date for the 12th repayment of the Republic of China's 20th Year Financial Short-Term Bonds and the 18th repayment of the Republic of China's 18th Year Military Reduction Bonds. I am delighted that you have all come to attend and observe. The total amount of the 20th Year Financial Short-Term Bonds issued was 80 million yuan. The first to eleventh principal payments have already been drawn. This time, we are drawing for the twelfth principal payment, with two bonds drawn, each for 80,000 yuan, totaling 160,000 yuan. This is equivalent to two per thousand of the total amount of the bonds issued. Therefore, the drawing method will be to use the same last three digits of the serial number as the winning bonds. The total amount of the 18th Year Military Reduction Bonds issued was 50 million yuan. The first to seventeenth principal payments have already been drawn. This time, we are drawing for the eighteenth principal payment, with one bond drawn for 500,000 yuan. This is equivalent to one percent of the total amount of the bonds issued. Therefore, the drawing method will be to use the same last two digits of the serial number as the winning bonds. The above-mentioned winning bonds, for the 20th Year Financial Short-Term Bonds, are scheduled to be paid starting on the 15th of this month, and for the 18th Year Military Reduction Bonds, are scheduled to be paid starting on the 31st of this month. The Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications will pay both principal and accrued interest together. Payments will be made in national currency, regardless of location. Please check the lottery slips and the bottom slips so that the drawing can be carried out."

Winning Numbers

After the chairman finished his report, the supervisor checked the lottery slips and the bottom slips. The lottery drawers then executed the drawing. Each time a slip was drawn, it was handed to the chairman for review and then to the supervisor for verification. Simultaneously, it was displayed on a placard and entered into the bottom slip by the registrar for verification. The winning numbers are recorded below: (1) Two bonds for the Republic of China 20th Year Financial Short-Term Bonds: (No. 443) (No. 533) (2) One bond for the Republic of China 18th Year Military Reduction Bonds: (No. 40) The Ministry of Finance will publish the above winning numbers in the newspaper.

Five Representatives from Silver and Money Industries Visited the Director of the Currency Department Yesterday

Requesting Permission for Free Transport of Cash in the Interior

According to the Guowen News Agency, due to the Ministry of Finance's regulations to prevent the export of silver, anyone transporting more than 1,000 silver dollars is required to obtain a passport. With the year-end settlement approaching, cash is tight everywhere, and the transfer of silver is frequent. On the 24th, a joint meeting of the executive committees of the Silver and Money Industries Associations was convened and decided to request the financial authorities to allow free transport of cash in non-port areas, as they are not related to exports. To alleviate the hardships of merchants, they requested that the Ministry of Finance exempt them from passport requirements. They immediately designated five representatives: Chen Guangfu, Chairman of the Bankers' Association; Qin Runqing, Chairman of the Money Dealers' Association; Bei Songsheng from the Bank of China; Tang Shoumin from the Bank of Communications; and Yu Zuoting from Hengxun Money Shop, to visit Xu Keting, Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance, at the Central Bank at approximately 10:00 AM yesterday. After presenting the opinions of the two associations, Xu stated that this matter must be handled according to procedures and requested the associations to draft a formal submission and submit it to the Ministry of Finance, which is likely to be approved. After the representatives left, they immediately supplemented the submission, which was jointly submitted by the two associations to the Ministry of Finance for processing.

After Resumption of Postal Service with Northeast China, Postal Rates Remain the Same as Before

Same as for Other Provinces and Cities

The issue of resuming postal service with Northeast China has been resolved. Mail to and from the four northeastern provinces will begin to be accepted starting on the 10th of this month. Regarding postal rates, a reporter learned from reliable sources yesterday that all postal fees for mail to the four northeastern provinces will still be charged according to previous practices, the same as for other provinces and cities. It is also reported that negotiations on the exchange of mail between inside and outside the customs have lasted for several months, repeatedly bordering on breakdown and were extremely difficult. The entire process involved technical solutions that did not involve signing or exchanging documents. The measures clearly stated that they did not involve political relations and were conducted under the principle of not recognizing the puppet regime. The representatives from the Kwantung Army involved in these negotiations were Fujiwara, Shibayama, and Iga, while the representatives from the Post Office were Gao Yu, Yin Li, and others. The Conte Rosso, sailing from Shanghai to Italy, is scheduled to depart on the 15th. By then, all matters should be settled, and he will depart on that ship. In short, all matters will be decided after President Sun returns south.

Attendees

A total of eight people will be flying to Guangzhou on this flight. The plane is scheduled to take off from Longhua Airport at 7:00 AM this morning and is expected to land in Wenzhou around 9:00 AM. Passengers will disembark to enjoy the scenery. It will arrive in Shantou at 12:30 PM that day, stay for one day, and then fly directly to Guangzhou at 9:00 AM on the morning of the 8th, arriving around 11:00 AM. Since the universal relief effort began collecting donations from wealthy individuals, it has gained the sympathy of many wealthy individuals, who have enthusiastically donated and committed to the universal relief effort. The number of donations has been high in recent days. All have sent representatives to the association to hand over the donations. China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Thoroughly Investigating Fairwind Anchoring Incident

Nearly Collided with Stone Embankment

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Fairwind vessel arrived at Laoyao, Haizhou, on the 27th of last month to load cargo. Because the Yongji and Tonghua vessels were docked at the wharf, the Fairwind was unable to dock and anchored outside the wave-breaking embankment near the foot of Malian Mountain in Lianyungang, waiting for the Yongji and others to leave before moving to the wharf. Unexpectedly, the waves were quite large that night, and the ship was hit by the waves. It drifted while anchored in the middle of the night, and no one on board knew. It was not until 3:30 AM on the 28th that the Fairwind had drifted near the wave-breaking embankment, and the ship was about to collide with the stone embankment. The crew discovered this and quickly stopped the ship. However, it had already drifted more than a nautical mile. They immediately requested the Dutch harbor construction engineering office and Kang Zhengji from the Longhai Railway to dispatch tugboats to the location to tow the Fairwind back to its original anchoring point. After the Yongji and others left, it then docked at the wharf to load cargo. A telegram was received yesterday stating that the ship can return to Shanghai today. The company is now conducting a thorough investigation.

Ministry of Finance Announces Measures for Revising the Tax on Ethyl Alcohol to a Unified Tax

Implemented on January 1st of the 24th Year of the Republic

Beneficial to Both Commercial and Tax Revenue

The Ministry of Finance considers ethyl alcohol to be an important industrial product. In the past, in order to prevent the blending of beverages, taxation was inevitably too high. Now, to alleviate business difficulties, ethyl alcohol will be subject to a unified tax. Provincial stamp tax and alcohol tax bureaus will stop collecting the tax, and the tax will be handled by unified tax agencies. This measure is beneficial to both commercial and tax revenue. The ministry yesterday instructed the Tax Affairs Department to publish and implement the Provisional Regulations for the Unified Tax on Ethyl Alcohol and the Collection Rules. The full text of the announcement and the regulations are recorded below:

Official Proclamation

Upon investigation, the collection of taxes on alcohol is handled by the provincial Stamp Tax Bureaus for Tobacco and Alcohol, in accordance with Article 3 of the Provisional Regulations for Taxes on Foreign Alcohol. The original tax rate, regardless of use, was set at twenty yuan per hundred catties for foreign alcohol. This was intended to prevent the adulteration of beverages and protect public health, but the tax rate was undeniably too high. Since the promulgation of regulations prohibiting alcohol adulteration, the harmful practice of adulterating beverages with alcohol can be expected to cease. The situation is different from before, and numerous merchants have repeatedly petitioned for a reduction in the tax rate. Considering the commercial situation in various regions and the current collection status, the Ministry of Finance recognizes that a change in the tax system is necessary. Because alcohol is related to industry and differs significantly from luxury goods, and because the original regulations stipulated collection from marketing stores, which led to disputes when taxes were paid and stamps affixed in one province and then transported to another, it is essential to differentiate based on use, appropriately reduce the tax rate, and implement a unified tax system. This is the only way to sympathize with merchants and benefit industry. Therefore, the Ministry has already drafted Provisional Regulations for the Unified Tax on Alcohol and Implementation Rules for Collection, which have been submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval and promulgation. The new regulations stipulate a tax rate of 13 cents in national currency per kilogram for ordinary alcohol. Assuming 4.545 kilograms per Imperial gallon, the tax is approximately 59 cents. Compared to the original tax rate of twenty yuan per hundred catties, this is equivalent to 26.3 cents per kilogram, a reduction of over half. For denatured alcohol used in industry, the tax is halved according to the customs import tax regulations, which is 6.5 cents in national currency per kilogram, a reduction of more than three-quarters compared to the old tax rate. All collection procedures will be handled by the unified tax authorities in each district. For alcohol manufactured domestically, the unified tax bureau in each district will dispatch personnel to the factory for collection. For imported alcohol, following the precedent for various unified taxes, the customs authorities will collect the unified tax in addition to the import duties at the currently established unified tax rate. Taxes will be uniformly levied based on the net packaged volume and stamps will be affixed. Alcohol that has completed the unified tax payment and has stamps affixed can be transported and sold in various provinces without being taxed again. The aforementioned revised measures will benefit both commerce and tax revenue. They are scheduled to take effect on January 1, 1935. In addition to instructing the provincial Stamp Tax Bureaus for Tobacco and Alcohol and the unified tax bureaus in each district to cease collection and take over the new system on schedule, the Customs Administration is ordered to instruct the Inspector General of Customs to inform all customs offices to comply accordingly. This proclamation is hereby issued for general information. Hereafter, all merchants manufacturing alcohol domestically, whether in the interior or concessions, shall comply with the regulations and apply for registration with the local unified tax authorities to facilitate the dispatch of personnel to the factory for collection. Alcohol imported or manufactured before the implementation of the unified tax that has not been reported for foreign alcohol tax shall also be reported to the unified tax authorities for inspection and stamp affixing before it can be sold. Failure to report or concealment will be treated as tax evasion and punished according to regulations. This proclamation.

Provisional Regulations

Article 1: All alcohol manufactured domestically or imported from foreign countries shall comply with these regulations and pay the unified alcohol tax. Article 2: The unified alcohol tax is a central national tax, collected by the General Tax District Bureaus and Unified Tax Management Offices under the General Affairs Department of the Ministry of Finance. Article 3: The unified alcohol tax rate shall be divided into two categories, A and B: (A) Ordinary alcohol: 13 cents in national currency per liter; (B) Denatured alcohol and wood alcohol (including light coconut wine and fusel oil): 6.5 cents in national currency per liter. Article 4: All alcohol imported from foreign countries shall, in addition to import duties collected by the customs authorities, be subject to the unified tax at the rates specified in the preceding article. Article 5: Alcohol on which the unified tax has been paid may be transported and sold in various provinces and regions without being taxed again. Article 6: All alcohol on which the unified tax has been paid shall have sufficient stamps affixed. A transport permit shall also be obtained for transportation. Article 7: Detailed regulations regarding the collection procedures, registration, inspection, and penalties for the unified alcohol tax shall be established separately. Article 8: These regulations shall take effect from the date of promulgation.
