Women's Garden

(This Year's Me) Special Issue

— Meng Jun

It's New Year again.

In the past, I dreaded the New Year, just as I disliked my annual birthday. I always felt it took something away, and what it left me wasn't exactly dazzling hope.

Now, I've changed that mindset. On the contrary, before the New Year even arrives, I find myself, like a child, with anticipation for the New Year, waiting for it. Because I want to settle accounts with the past and also start some new plans.

My plans don't have anything extravagant, but they are a solid spur for myself. I want to use them as a yardstick to measure whether the days of this year are wasted.

Naturally, I'm not a member of the leisure class. I have to spend eight hours a day to earn a living. I don't use work to kill time. But the responsibility of the era rests on everyone's shoulders, and I'm only willing to appropriately shoulder the portion I can bear.

First, I am planning with friends to set up a nursery, in Nanjing, where there isn't one yet. The goal is to give large groups of women time to participate in social activities and become a part of advancing the times. It is necessary to find ways to reduce their burden of childcare. We also know that the few nurseries can only help a small number of women, but using facts as propaganda, the impact will not be small.

Second, running remedial schools: We are all a group who have neither money nor philanthropists or high-ranking officials to rely on. All we have are some spare time and enthusiasm. Remedial schools are based on these objective conditions. So our plan is to rent one or two rooms in a peasant community or near a small factory, gather thirty to fifty poor women, and we ourselves will be the teachers. Naturally, we also hope that through the teacher-student relationship, they can give us some practical lessons, and we can also help them more.

Third, we also have a group, which was just organized last year, and it has not yet reached a sound stage. 1935 will make it gradually sound, until it can shoulder greater and more responsibilities.

Furthermore: My knowledge and ability are not enough. Moreover, the times are progressing day by day. How to prevent myself from being knocked down by the times in this continuous progress, and how to enrich myself to adapt to the work I am willing to undertake, this is also one of my plans for this year.

First, theoretical understanding is the compass for action. Without theory as a basis, work is blind. In China, where even translation work is scarce, not being able to read foreign language books means almost no opportunity to receive new theories. Therefore, mastering a foreign language has become an urgent need for me personally.

Second, reading and writing: In addition to ordinary magazines, systematic reading is to enrich myself and help me act more correctly. Writing is also in my plan.

Due to space limitations, I can only end this briefly.

January 2, 1935, in Nanjing.

— Cai Muhui

This morning, I went to the office. As soon as I stepped out of the elevator, someone said, "HAPPY NEW YEAR." Naturally, I had to reply with a "HAPPY NEW YEAR," even though in my heart, I really didn't have the slightest interest in celebrating the New Year. Entering the room, I saw many mails piled on the desk. After opening and reading them one by one, I felt very ashamed, because I haven't sent New Year's cards to relatives and friends for several years.

In the past, when the New Year was approaching, I did spend a lot of time racking my brains to print New Year cards and such things. I also often talked with my sisters about the plans for the coming year by the candlelight on New Year's Eve. But in recent years, because I have had too much life experience of "(eight or nine times things happen unexpectedly, only two or three times things conform to the plan)," I have lost the interest in printing New Year cards and discussing plans. A few days ago, Ms. Zi Jiu asked me to write a section on "(This Year's Me)," but I refused for this reason. Last night, she specified in the phone that I should write about going abroad, and because I couldn't find any more reasons to refuse, tonight I have to lock myself in a cold room and write a few words that I didn't originally intend to write.

Anyway, Ms. Zi Jiu didn't say that I had to make a report at the end of the year. Even if my plan cannot be realized, I don't have to apologize to the readers, so I will boldly write on. Otherwise...

My colleagues, because I have been doing mechanical work for seven or eight years, really want to give me a chance to go out and get some fresh air. In the past few months, they have been racking their brains to plan travel expenses and contact schools for me. I will probably be able to go around the end of summer or early autumn. Although I haven't expressed anything to them, I am very grateful for their kindness in my heart. They have scheduled a little more than a year for my trip, and the travel route is first to the United States and then to Europe. In New York City, I can probably spend a few months as a student, but I don't have the ambition to get a degree. I just want to choose one or two more interesting courses according to my own interests. During this trip, as long as I can travel to more places, observe the actual lives of people in various countries more, and have more opportunities to come into contact with various ideas, my own wishes will be satisfied. My colleagues and friends naturally have many more extravagant hopes. They often tell me this and that, but in this short period of time, I'm afraid there are quite a few things that cannot be done, so I'd better not say them now.

A few days ago, a friend said to me, "(Would you like us to prepare a large batch of stupid questions for you? That's what you will often need to answer after you go to the United States. We Americans are best at asking stupid questions, and people without experience can easily be embarrassed by them.)" I think her words are right. Although I have never been abroad, I have been embarrassed by Americans many times. Therefore, in the seven or eight months before going abroad, I may have to spend more of my spare time preparing stupid answers to stupid questions.

— Bai Wei

Disease and poverty can destroy a person's entire life: everything of mine has been ruined by illness. But this year, I always want to turn over from the sea of ​​suffering from illness and appear in a healthy posture.

If I could be on camera: I would like to play a particularly individual and most tragic role among the bankrupt peasants in the countryside and the unemployed poor in the city. Because I have the passion to act in tragedies, I have the (theatrical personality) to laugh and cry suddenly, and can shout out the most profound sorrow for them.

If I could be a director: I would like to draw a strictly armed boundary line on the same world stage, and on one side perform the vampires of the colony, their ferocious faces, sinister means, violent and terrifying authority, and extravagant lives;) on the other side, perform the forced extraction, slaughter, and people struggling in hunger, death, and cries, their scene in the dark hell. Then, from the body of each toiling and oppressed person, draw a glistening thread of blood and sweat directly to the vampires, turning it into piles of gold coins for them to enjoy, to be used to supply the Second World War and create more colonies and more slaves.

Making the stage such a strong contrast, a realistic photograph, let the audience know who should seize the guns that draw the boundary and use them to fight their own enemy, the imperialists!

But can I realize this kind of desire? To talk about this year's me, I have to settle accounts with the past me: I have been dragged down by six years of terrible illness, making me like a living corpse that has not been buried. My miserable life is unbelievable. The spring before last, I locked myself in my room and fell into bed for five days, and no one knew about it. The first person to discover that I was seriously ill was the young eldest daughter of Mr. Wang Zaoshi's family. She opened my door, woke me up, borrowed money to take me to the Red Cross Hospital for treatment, and then gambled and won money to buy me medicine. Last autumn, my fierce illness came in succession and could not be cured. Just when I was in danger of letting it kill me, I unexpectedly received some money from a kind stranger to save my life.

My life was saved, but the disease has penetrated deep into my bones and I still cannot move. I am heavily in debt and my life is miserable. I have not been able to buy a book or magazine for three or four years. In this way, what else can I do while alive? When the creditors force me to escape, I am afraid that the newspapers this year will have the news of "(Bai Wei jumping into the sea to commit suicide)." At that time, I, who am often rumored by tabloids, don't know what tricks the tabloids will use to spread rumors about me?

— Jun

I believe that people cannot do whatever they want, on the contrary, the environment makes you do what it wants. This may be mechanical objectivism, but I think it is closer to the truth. According to my experience, a person's ability to act always cannot withstand the compulsion of the environment!

(This year's me), I think it will be the same as in previous years. Even if I have some plans, I will always hit a wall with the environment when implementing them! So I don't want to talk about any annual plans. However, at the beginning of this year, I have to go back to my hometown. This is indeed a big change in my personal life. On this eve of parting, let's talk about my feelings about living in Shanghai for the past few years.

The only means of production I rely on to make a living in Shanghai is the G-pen nib, Globe brand ink, and Kaiming manuscript paper. I, who have no literary reputation in the cultural world, can only be a (book translator) who changes the appearance of Japanese goods into domestic goods under the (cultural and commercial public)'s package. Although the wages are very limited, my family of several people will not starve to death. But recently, the publishing industry is in a panic, especially the native culture is in the limelight. The smart (cultural and commercial public) seized the opportunity to change careers, and as a result, I became an unemployed person who cannot even be exploited. In fact, it is common to starve to death and freeze to death in Shanghai due to unemployment. Just thinking about this makes me shudder!

However, I am not disappointed because of this. I believe that this situation will not last long. The world will one day be free from unemployment panic. This year's me is only looking forward to this day coming sooner!

— Guo Zhenyi

Like such a small me, floating and sinking in the sea of ​​life, year after year, not worthy of saying anything about this year. However, the whip of experience always whips people to recall the past and look forward to the future.

Reading for a diploma and writing for fame seem to be a common phenomenon. Experience tells me that in order to enrich my life, in addition to being tempered by life, I need to read more valuable books myself. This year, I hope to write some articles that are harmless to people and buy some books that are beneficial to myself.

Saving the country, running social undertakings, and behaviors that win social praise, and actions that are praised by people, seem to be the aspirations of those who consider themselves extraordinary. Experience tells me that in this deformed society, these are all tools used by "(smart people)" to deceive ordinary people. This year, I hope to recognize the direction of the history of human evolution and do things in a way that does not violate the trend of this great era.

Entering the political stage to increase one's prestige and participating in the women's movement to show off one's talent seem to be the outlets that some people recognized in the past. Experience tells me that these are mostly the selfish thoughts of individualists and have nothing to do with the masses of women and the suffering masses. This year, I hope to broaden my horizons, see through the core of things, and develop a courageous and progressive outlook on life. With correct consciousness, do some small work that people are unwilling to do and disdain to do.

— Guan Lu

The New Year is here. According to the general Chinese custom, the New Year should be laughed at. Crying can bring about a year of success. But how do I cry? If I am an old woman, when I laugh, a tooth falls out of my mouth, I can be comforted: this chaotic and poor time has reduced my age by one year. If I am a young daughter, when I laugh on New Year's morning and娇滴滴(jiāodīdi-) call out "(Mom)," a piece of candy or a glutinous rice ball will immediately fall into my mouth. If I now have a wealthy gentleman husband, then on the eve of the New Year, I dress up, put on high heels, twist my waist a couple of times, walk 咯哒咯哒(gē dá gē dá) to my husband who is leaning on the sofa smoking a pipe, and (拍) (pāi)print a red lip print on his cheek, then purse my lips and glance at him, 扑哧(pūchī) send the sound and appearance together into his pipe. He puts his arms around my waist, and I take the opportunity to act coquettishly:

"(Honey, I will always belong to you, and I will never associate with any boyfriends in the future. But you are not allowed to take money to spend on other women. Tonight, hee hee, I will好好地(hǎohāodì)......)."

In this way, at least my New Year's mahjong expenses will not be a problem.

But I am nothing, I have nothing. All I have is my own labor and a few iron nails brought back from the labor market. Then, don't laugh and cry? How dare I! In the current society that tramples on women, in a social system that only supports women selling their bodies and does not allow women to sell their labor, we are in need of hard struggle. Now, we can neither laugh nor cry. We must work hard to find companions and transform the "(human flesh market)" for women into a labor market.

This non-laughing and non-crying is my New Year!

— Yao Huilian

I am a freshman in college and got married on New Year's Day last year, so I could not continue my studies. My husband is a member of the bourgeoisie, and the condition for him to marry me is my "(beauty)."

My position in the family can be regarded as "(young mistress)." I live in a three-story foreign house, wear silk and satin, and ride in a car. In short, the material enjoyment is extremely luxurious. If I had no knowledge, then I might as well bury my life in this turbid air.

But I have now decided to divorce him. After the divorce, I plan to work as a female worker in a factory, wanting to develop the ability to be self-reliant, and on the one hand, to fulfill my long-held wishes.

Because a person who is simply a "(biological person)" can be said to be an incomplete person. Only by being a "(social person)" can one have the meaning of a person and be considered a complete person.

The life of a "(young mistress)" is, at best, a typical woman of a virtuous mother and good wife. To put it plainly, it is a victim of traditional concepts and social systems. Because in this way, the husband's will is my will, and I cannot have my own free will. In this way, I am equivalent to an accessory of the husband. In other words, I am just his sexual tool. But I have innate freedom and will and should transform my current environment.

Going to work in a factory as a worker, although workers in the eyes of ordinary capitalists are simply treated like cattle and horses, workers are still more decent than they are, who sit in cars, live in foreign houses, and marry concubines with the profits generated by the workers' sweat and blood. Therefore, I want to go to work, to preach, to teach... to make people realize what workers are. I think this kind of obligation should also be fulfilled.

In a nutshell, this year's me is not an ornament of the bourgeoisie, but a completely independent and free person, and I also want to help others succeed in becoming completely independent and free people.

— Yin

First of all, please allow me to use a few words to explain the past me. In this regard, borrowing a famous saying often used by a certain gentleman is enough, namely: "(Unemployment, unemployment, the third one is still unemployment.)"

For many years, I, who have been crushed by unemployment and have become a "(career insulated body)," will not have much promise this year! Fortunately, at the end of last year, a friend told me that a famous foreign university in this city has a special vocational guidance department, which specializes in vocational guidance. Many Chinese and foreign scholars are engaged in guidance, and many young Chinese men and women have also chosen this department as a lifelong career and started to immerse themselves in research there with four years of university time.

For me, this is more practical than the news of the Buddha's rebirth. Therefore, this year's me, the first step is to be like a Muslim going on a pilgrimage to Mecca, regardless of wading through mountains and rivers, I also want to meet these vocational guidance experts who are saviors of the unemployed. Even if I can't get in and see the great experts, I will also visit one or two of their disciples and grandchildren. If, fortunately, the first step (unemployment) is resolved, everything will be no problem for this year's me. If I am lucky enough to get a small prize, then I will find a way to publish the secret in the newspapers or magazines to the unemployed comrades.

— Jingbo

I especially feel that this year's active New Year has a strong enlightening power, a time-dividing critique, how the present and the future give me a kind of necessary self-consciousness.

In any case, detachment from practice is a critical illness of life! Especially for me, a woman who is oppressed! Surrounding me are: the threat of poverty and illness; the humble temptation of quiet enjoyment; the tenderness of love like a net; the unprincipled empty talk life of intellectuals. If I am negligent or slack, it is obvious and easy that if I am not destroyed by poverty and illness, I will be crushed under the wheels of the times.

Hidden in the subtle weaknesses and ignorance in life, if not criticized and overcome, will inevitably develop into the cause of falling at some point in time. That's right, if the threat of reality unconsciously泛滥(fànlàn) in my heart, temptation and indulgence will take advantage of the situation; what is the conclusion of my life? How terrible this is!

From the past to yesterday, from yesterday to today, the history of the fall and rise of many figures cannot be regarded as accidental, but is precisely a mirror of our lives. — Xian

The cold wind gusts, blowing away all the stale things of twenty-three years.

The New Year dances with the symbol of hard work, singing the song of progress, and walks out of the crowded crowd.

The New Year, this singable and laudable, joyful and encouraging New Year, she is pregnant with the melting light of spring and the power of life! This power is the driving force behind everything on earth. Ah, New Year, she will push this earth to walk towards the bright road! Run over the muddy fields and walk on the flat avenue!

The New Year will also push the women of the earth and push them to the broad society. Let them expand the things of the family into the things of the society; simplify and specialize. Organize public childcare, public canteens, sewing, weaving, dyeing companies... etc. Everyone does what they can and engages in the work they want to do; dedicate the whole self to mankind and serve the entire mankind.

Women, take your supreme love and love the public, don't just love your husband and son! Sacrifice your supreme ability for the public; don't sacrifice your precious mind and body only for your lover!

Because I am a woman, I hope that when women are pushing the wheel of the times in the New Year, they will all move forward with a clamor!

The hope for women is also the hope for myself. From now on: I want to take off this silk robe that binds my actions, throw away these pointed high heels that hinder my steps, cut off this foot-long, tortuous and not straightforward troublesome hair, and wash away the grease and powder that contaminates my pure skin. Nakedly be a new woman and a new me in 1935!

— Pu Shunqing

I am studying law, currently practicing law, and also a lover of literature. On this New Year's Day morning of the 24th year, I planned what I should do this year: Now I summarize and write it below:

(1) At least ten famous works of law and literature should be read carefully this year to enrich the tools of work.

(2) Compile two law books and two dramas this year. (Because although I am a person who studies law, I also love drama.)

(3) In my lawyer's duties, I will do my best to help oppressed women and recover their legal rights.

(4) Last year, my friend Lawyer Chen Yunxian and I planned to set up a women's voluntary legal advisory department in the firm to solve legal problems for women with financial difficulties. I hope this can be realized this year.

(5) This year, I am willing to help a thousand women gain the legal knowledge they deserve.

I hope to implement the above simple work plan without any discount, so as not to fail this year's me. Now I have written it out to warn myself and earnestly ask my loving friends to encourage me!

New Year's Day of the 24th year in Shanghai

— Yang Yu

All human activities cannot be separated from starting from the individual or society. Only when individuals live a stable life can we talk about social efforts; therefore, for this year's me, the prerequisite is still to calculate the livelihood of this year, and at the same time, my personal attitude towards life and the direction of being a person must also be determined. Recalling the five years since I left school life, I stepped into this colorful society. I have been a school teacher and an editor, but five years of experience and the lessons society has taught me are that I don't understand society and can't adapt to society. Using the theory of being a person obtained from books for more than ten years to deal with society is really not in line with the way of survival in the current society. People are singing loudly about saving the country with personality and being fair and selfless, and the posture is hard and upright, but I know that this is just a means of the superiors to the subordinates and the big figures to the small figures. And I have not thoroughly understood this truth, and stubbornly, directly, and foolishly, as a result, I am farther and farther away from society. When it comes to what movement, people's brand is hung high and for a long time, holding meetings, giving speeches, writing articles, and talking about liberation, making a shocking noise, but I, without understanding that this is an occasion to create a position for myself, did not know how to be opportunistic or suspect in advance, so people thought I was stupid and foolish. This year's me, what attitude should I take in the direction of walking? This question was carefully considered on the eve of the New Year, and finally it was decided that this year's trend of being a person is still to take the stupid road. The first is to strengthen the individual's personality and maintain an independent spirit. To be able to break into and out of society, regardless of losses, hardships, and being fooled, strive to struggle. The second is that beyond the small self, do not forget the big self. If I am myself, can't I express my personality and implement my views in the big self, then wouldn't my struggle be meaningless? My comrades urge me and her to continue our cause and expand our organization, the Female Voice Society. This is really the key point in my plan this year. As long as society gives a glimmer of light, so that this stupid person has the opportunity to work hard, this year's me will not be in vain in these three hundred and sixty-five days.

— Zhu Yongli

I am a sixteen-year-old girl. The year I came to Shanghai from Hunan, I happened to encounter Japan starting a war against us, so my father became unemployed. Later, when my family's life became impossible, I was introduced to a cotton mill to work. After working for more than three months, I only received two yuan in wages, so I stopped doing it. Then I was introduced to a factory to work. Although the wages in this factory were very small, the work was very light and the time was not much, so my father taught me to read in the evening and I worked during the day. This way, I supplemented the family's life and continued until now.

I know that we young people need to maintain our lives and acquire knowledge at the same time, so from this year on, I will continue my past plan, working and studying at the same time. Naturally, there is no better way other than this. But I know that reading is not just about recognizing a few characters, but about understanding our own problems; because I am a young person, and those modern ladies are also young people. Why do they have the opportunity to go to school: I don't know how many young women like me are in China now. Why don't they all have the opportunity to go to school, and only a few modern ladies can go to school?

After a certain Luo, a former speculator in the gold market, dumped gold, the financial chips suddenly became loose. Later, buyers became active as they saw low prices, and shorts also covered their positions. Unfavorable Rumors Spread, Cotton Market Decline Becomes More Evident

The cotton market weakened due to a reactionary fall of four rupees after the rise in Indian cotton, which further weakened confidence. Rumors circulated in the market that the Zhengzhou cotton market was loosening, and simultaneously, gold prices softened, exchange rates lengthened, and buyers decreased. However, large holders still refused to release their large quantities. In the afternoon, rumors spread that several factories might shut down, which would inevitably reduce their future demand for raw materials.

Zheng Biao cotton fell by one or two jiao before the market opened due to the reactionary fall of three or four rupees in Indian cotton. Gold prices continued to fall, exchange rates lengthened, and there was ample Northwest cotton in storage, most of which had not yet been exported. Due to tightening credit conditions, market prices loosened, resulting in fewer buyers. Prices for all months fell by five fen to one jiao and a half. In the afternoon, short positions were covered, resulting in a slight recovery, but after two or three auctions, rumors spread widely in the market that several factories would implement shutdowns, further weakening market sentiment. Prices for all months fell by another five fen, except for distant months, which rose slightly by five fen. US Agricultural Policy Unchanged, Cotton Market Quietly Firm

Yesterday, the New York American cotton market opened quietly. Before the President's speech to Congress, the market was stable, with minimal price fluctuations. Disappointing news from Liverpool prompted local and Indian traders to take profits. However, other traders and foreign firms continued to buy. After President Roosevelt announced that the government's agricultural policy would remain unchanged, the market remained quiet. At the close, there was some buying in distant months, with prices rising three points. Spot prices remained unchanged, while futures prices rose two to four points. English cotton was sold by Indian traders, while local traders bought due to firmness in Alexandria and falling silver prices. Spot prices rose two points, and futures prices rose two or three points. Indian cotton initially weakened due to sales by European exporters, then strengthened due to short covering, and finally softened again due to sales by futures traders. Pingguoer fell 3.25 rupees, Aomula fell 3.5 rupees, and Bairoxi fell 4 rupees. (Reported on the 4th)

According to a Bombay dispatch, the opening forecast for Bairoxi cotton on the 5th is 240 rupees, down 1.5 rupees from the previous day's close.

Another New York dispatch on the 4th reported on the cotton market for the week: Trading on the New York Cotton Exchange was limited last week due to the New Year holiday and general anticipation of developments in Washington. The general business climate is good, which should stabilize prices, and there is some buying from traders. At the same time, foreign cotton prices have also risen, with foreign countries such as Liverpool, Japan, and Bombay all increasing their purchases. However, price increases are hindered by long covering and government sales, but supply remains thin. The price difference between New York and Liverpool has widened since the publication of the reduced estimate of East Indian cotton production. Moreover, the tight supply of comparable grades abroad further fuels excitement about increased export demand. Domestic hoarders remain firm, but it is widely believed that a small portion of the goods, currently pledged for 12 cents, or private production, will be sold when the March price reaches 13 cents or above.

Grain and Flour Fall Sharply, Minor Rebound

The flour market was weak then stable yesterday morning after opening. Quotations for foreign wheat from Chicago, Canada, and other places were about four to eight fen higher. At the opening, due to the large drop the previous day, people inside and outside the industry could not help but wait and see. The opening price for the current month was as low as four jiao, seven fen, and seven li and a half. However, as it approached the distant period, because the millers' hedging had stopped and there were no heard offers of spot wheat, people were steady, and bidding gradually became steady. In addition, the market filled in the gaps. The market atmosphere became more stable. When the afternoon market opened, the atmosphere was tight for the current month due to swap transactions. Large outside accounts continued to take in distant periods, so although factories put up orders, sentiment remained good. It was found that foreign wheat chips were only one-tenth or two-tenths of what they were in previous years. If there is no continued determination later, the trend will still seem stable. As a result, the current month was up two and a half li, February was up one and a half fen, March was up one fen and two and a half li, April was up one and a half fen, May was up one fen and seven and a half li, and June was up two fen and seven and a half li.

The wheat market was generally stable. The quotation for foreign wheat was only about four or eight fen higher. After the opening price, the current month was very stable due to the scarcity of spot goods. The distant period was stable due to poor delivery of households. Each transaction was still active, and the price was still hovering. When the afternoon market opened, transactions in each month became light again. In the current month, merchants slightly increased their purchases due to insufficient spot wheat, and the price was one or two fen higher. There were very few openings for distant periods, and there were few ups and downs. As a result, the current month was two fen, February was one fen, and March was three fen. Nothing else was heard. Spot wheat was not opened all day because the factory's appetite had not moved.

Chicago wheat: Buyers are waiting to see when prices rise. The Far East's need for Australian wheat is extremely active. Argentina exports small batches of wheat. Foreign Rice and Indica Rice Sales Active Again

Another Boatload of Rice Arrives

Yesterday, the indica rice market was affected by the upstream winter drought, which made transportation inconvenient and increased costs while reducing supplies. However, the appetite on this street increased greatly, and the mainland also continued to purchase. Yesterday's trading was even more active. 6,600 bags of Hunan rice, 1,537 bags of Shashi rice, and 100 bags of Wuyuan rice were sold. In addition to more than 1,000 bags going to the mainland, all were handled by this street. As demand exceeds supply, prices rose step by step by five fen to one jiao.

Foreign rice has been arriving continuously in recent days. Yesterday, another boatload of rice, approximately 20,000 bags, arrived on the Taikoo Jiaxing wheel. The market inventory is gradually thickening, and orders continue to arrive. Subsequent batches will also arrive continuously. The market should be flat and soft. However, although this guest's appetite is fragrant these days, this street is still greedy, so the current rice can still stand firm. Yesterday, 8,000 bags of Saigon broken machine rice were sold. Fabric and Wool Market Conditions Are Greatly Different from the Past

Woolen fabrics and wool textiles: According to past practice, after the end of the national lunar year, there is often a large sales market for overcoat woolen fabrics, and the Sichuan gang also often opens spring goods. At present, it is very different from the past. The Sichuan gang does not move at all. Overcoat woolen fabric street sales are sluggish, and the price of goods has fallen and not risen. The capital of the colleagues has become tight. Looking at the accounts at the end of the national lunar year, it is more than half as good as in previous years. In addition, the Western clothing gang's bank checks are full of refunds. Even the goods purchased one or two months ago are often requested to be returned because there is no money when the accounts are received. In short, the dire situation of the market is very different from the past. It is even worse than the "January 28th" Shanghai battle.

Shen Bao Local Supplement Amateur Weekly

New Year Special Issue (2)

Chinese Song and Dance in the Past Year

— Feng Yongtang

(1) A General Discussion of Song and Dance (Business Perspective)

In the past two or three years, the Chinese song and dance scene has already embarked on a path of decline. Bare thighs and exposed breasts are no longer easy to sell, and lewd songs and seductive dances have also nearly lost their appeal. Song and dance troupes that go to various places to perform mostly return in miserable defeat. If the song and dance troupe owners are wealthy young masters, they can still afford to lose their capital, but if they are some wandering (performers), they will even lose their (costumes) after a business failure. The situation of song and dance troupes has not changed much to this day. Generally speaking, this year's song and dance scene is still shrouded in an atmosphere of recession. Several famous song and dance troupes have not earned much money in their few performances. Now, I might as well briefly mention a few song and dance performances in Shanghai.

First, I want to talk about the Plum Blossom Troupe. The (Plum Blossom Troupe) is a well-known name in the song and dance scene. Two years ago, Plum Blossom was equally impoverished, but since returning from a tour in Singapore and other places in Southeast Asia, the troupe owner has moved into a Western-style house and drives a car. (In Southeast Asia, song and dance are still relatively rare. The reason why the Plum Blossom Troupe could make money this time is because overseas Chinese still don't see enough of bare thighs. But this year, the (Shanghai Technical Song and Dance Troupe) went to Southeast Asia, and the situation was a bit different.) This year, Plum Blossom also held several performances, but the business situation was not very good. In May, they performed so-called (1934-style song and dance) at the Jincheng Grand Theater. The advertisements boasted loudly, saying: (Beautiful women fill the eyes, with thousands of charming postures, once you appreciate the sound, you won't taste meat for three months. If you want to explore the heart of the plum blossom, now is the time!) All kinds of fragrant words and seductive phrases are enough to scare people away. Who with artistic cultivation would dare to come and learn? The (featured play) this time was (Love School), a ridiculous and fanciful song and dance drama, which did not attract much attention. At the end of July, following the Xinhua Opera Troupe, the Plum Blossom Troupe performed at the Xinguang Theater again. This performance lasted for a considerable period, from July 27th to August 13th, a total of 18 days, and the program was changed several times. Although there were many spectators, they were not very enthusiastic, and the business was not very prosperous. The reason why they could perform for so many days was due to other reasons. It turned out that the business of movie theaters was generally sluggish during the summer vacation. At that time, Xinguang was planning to) close for the summer). Since song and dance could still attract a portion of erotic audiences and there was money to be made, there was nothing wrong with maintaining it for a few more days. This performance of Plum Blossom, whether in terms of talent or program, was on a larger scale than the one at Jincheng. In order to make everyone understand the song and dance situation a little more, I would like to introduce it well. The actors who appeared on stage this time, in addition to the (starring) (hot girl) Miss Xu Canying, also included Zhang Qi, Zhang Xianlin, Cai Yiming, Fan Lixiang, Pan Wenxia, Pan Wenjuan, Qian Zhongxiu, Jia Qiuyun, and Weng Lanxue, among others. The so-called (Five Tiger Generals, Four Diamond Warriors) were among them. In terms of program, there were (the latest great creation) (A Spring Dream), (exquisite and unparalleled) (Playing), (rich and fragrant) (Yang Guifei), (The Scandalous History of Xuan Palace), (witty and stimulating) (Backstage), (immortal) (Seven Emotions). These were all featured plays, brought out one after another. Plum Blossom can be said to have pulled out all the goods in the world, such as a graceful dance, a charming dance, (Wave Dance), (Jade Rabbit Dance), (Grass Skirt Dance), (Javanese Girl), (Black and White Dance), (Spanish Dance), (Charleston Dance), (Tap Dance), (Lia Dance), (Butterfly Dance), (Clang Dance), Sailor Dance)······ such as (Night Fragrance), (Spring is Full of the Garden), (Blooming Flowers), (Flowers Bloom For You), (Fruit of Love), (Spring Night Song), (Butterfly Shadows), (I Can't Forget You), (Playing Dragon and Phoenix), (Love Companion), (New Drizzle), (Double Flight), (Pleasure of Youth), (Pursuit), (In the Night Garden), (White Powder and Black Paint), (Marry a Warrior)······ these, whether dance, song, or drama, are all fragrant and charming. Just hearing these names is fragrant and charming enough!

Not long ago, Plum Blossom also performed in a small theater in this city, but this has never attracted people's attention, and the scale is also very small, so I don't plan to mention it here anymore.

The Xinhua Opera Troupe also held a so-called (the greatest song and dance performance in history for the first time) from July 20th to 23rd, and also pulled in many female stars for (guest appearances). The grand occasion at that time can be imagined. In terms of talent, if Misses Yuan Meiyun, Li Lili, Bai Hong, Hu Jia, Li Mingjian, Cang Yinqiu, and Jiang Manli are all very talented, and if they can get good guidance, they can indeed have a future in (song) and (dance). Xu Jian, Yu Hua, Ye Ying, and Ouyang Feili of Xinhua Society are all smart girls and have a lot of potential: it's a pity that they haven't cherished their talents and haven't gone in the direction of new singing and new dancing, which is inevitably a loss. For example, this public performance of Xinhua lacks new goods, and most of the programs are leftovers inherited from the Mingyue Society. What (Swan Dance), (Milky Way Dance), (Bubble Dance)······ what (Flower of Love), (Night Fragrance), (Four Angels), (Physical Exercise), (Fair Trade), (Returning Home in Wind and Rain), (Modern Love), (Secrets of Courtship), (Under the Sword), (Special Express), etc., we cannot give them too high an evaluation, although some of them, such as the children's song and dance drama (Special Express), are relatively worth watching. Naturally, this time was relatively marketable.

At the same time as Plum Blossom's performance at Xinguang (early August), Xinhua and the Qunyan Song and Dance Troupe (led) by (Oriental Locke) Shao Zhuanglin also jointly performed at the Guangdong Grand Theater in Hongkou. Although a few new people were added this time, the program was still the same old stuff, and the business was also very ordinary, so I don't plan to explain it here anymore. In addition, there are some small song and dance troupes, such as (Yinhua) (Mingming) (Huaguang) (Taohua) (Jimei) (Lengyan), etc., either performing in amusement parks such as the Great World or second- and third-class theaters in this city, or going to other places to wander for a while, but none of them have improved much, so there is no need to talk about them here. In short, if the song and dance scene does not open up new avenues, they will not be able to break through the current atmosphere of recession and achieve something.

(2) The Entry and Exit of Song and Dance in the Film Industry

The fact that song and dance does not have much of a future is a clear fact, which cannot be avoided. It is a natural result for the song and dance scene to run to the film industry and broadcasting industry to cultivate its power for its own future. I will not talk about the activities of the song and dance scene in broadcasting for the time being; in the film industry, after the American Warner Company's (Forty-Second Street) and other song and dance films made money, the domestic song and dance film (Human Fairy) was also able to make a little money. As a result, some people in the song and dance scene organized their own film companies to shoot films, and some joined film companies and became stars. For example, some people in the Plum Blossom Troupe organized another Plum Blossom Film Company and started shooting (Song of the Rose), and also made a joke of trying to be clever but failing. Originally, the protagonist of the film, Pan Wenxia, was unknown. In order to attract attention, the host arranged a fake lawsuit, offered a reward, and made a lot of noise, which was known to everyone in the city. In addition, many people from the Mingyue Society, Xinhua Society, and Plum Blossom Troupe have also gone to the screen. Bai Hong and Li Mingjian of the Mingyue Society have already performed in (Human Fairy), and Yin Ying has performed in (Physical Exercise); in addition to Pan Wenxia, Pan Wenjuan, Xu Canying, and Fan Lixiang of the Plum Blossom Troupe have all played important roles in films. Many members of the Xinhua Society have played supporting roles and moving scenery in several films of Tianyi this year. Huang, the owner of the Plum Blossom Troupe, also has a plan to equip a sound machine and take the troupe to foreign countries to shoot films at any time, which is currently underway.

The advance of song and dance into the film industry did not start today. Three or four years ago, Wang Renmei, Li Lili, Hu Jia, etc. had already jumped onto the screen, and even earlier there was Li Minghui, but at that time it was not just performing song and dance films. In the future, domestic song and dance films may form a trend, but this also depends on the content and technology, especially the technology. Without Hollywood's huge capital, some crudely made things, hoping to be as marketable as (Forty-Second Street), I'm afraid it won't happen, right? The audience can only be deceived once. From this point of view, the future of Chinese song and dance films is also very bleak.

(3) Also a Major Event

Speaking of this, I remembered another interesting thing. Everyone probably still remembers the song star contest on the Big Evening News this summer, right? Here, I'm going to talk about it. This election took more than a month, and the voters can be said to have been very enthusiastic. Every week, the election results were announced, and Bai Hong of the Mingyue Society and Zhou Xuan of the Xinhua Society received the most votes. As a result, Bai Hong was elected first with 9,103 votes, Zhou Xuan was elected second with 8,876 votes, and Wang Manjie was elected third with 8,854 votes. These three are the (three major song stars) we are familiar with now. These little girls, who usually don't attract much attention, actually have tens of thousands of people supporting them, which is a bit strange, but maybe it's really because they sing well? I have to admit that their voices are quite promising: but I think they don't necessarily really understand music. I once saw someone satirize the (three major song stars), saying that at a certain amusement park held in Xu Garden on Kang Nao Tu Road, there was an English song solo program by one of the (three major song stars). Two blue-eyed gentlemen in the audience stood up and left their seats as soon as they heard the singing. This is probably not because the two foreign gentlemen didn't understand English songs, right? Undoubtedly, this is their lack of understanding of singing. They should study in more depth and never regard some currently popular vulgar modern songs as treasures, because these things have no high value in music (their dances are also of little value).

(4) Final Remarks

Speaking of this, I must add a point about the future of Chinese new song and dance. Song, dance, and song and dance dramas are undoubtedly necessary, but they are definitely not what Chinese song and dance can currently fill. We need song and dance with new content and forms. We don't need song and dance that sells bare thighs and breasts, and sells sensuality. All lewd lyrics and seductive tunes, grotesque shapes and strange forms, are poisons that anesthetize and harm young people. They should have no place in real song and dance and should be eliminated. Real song and dance should not just imitate a little bit of the superficiality of foreign jazz music and a little bit of foreign seductive dance postures. It should have a higher level of musical foundation, more complex melody coordination, more powerful and beautiful body postures that can represent a national character, and collective forms of dance postures. I hope that people who work hard in song and dance will improve or create new Chinese song and dance from this other direction!

Recent Photo of Song and Dance Star Ms. Li Mingjian

Chinese Film in the Past Year

— Ms. Xia Zhende

There have been particularly many events in the film industry this year, making a detailed account impossible within this short space. Now, I only want to briefly describe a few of the most important aspects and prominent issues.

(1) Overview of the Film Industry: Following the global wave of economic recession, the Chinese film industry has gradually reached a critical point of decline over the past year. Whether in terms of film companies or theaters, most have entered a state of struggle. Let's start with the film companies. The Chinese film industry is concentrated in Shanghai, where Mingxing, Lianhua, Tianyi, and Yihua are the giants not only of Shanghai but of the entire Chinese film industry, as we all know. The business conditions of these companies have always been kept secret and never disclosed to the outside world, but we can infer a general idea from the box office performance of their films. After the success of "Sister Flowers" this year, Mingxing Company seemed more active, establishing a "Revival Comrades Association" on April 1st to plan for revival and debt repayment. However, Mingxing's other films this year, such as "Two Against One," "A Woman's Enemy," "Youth Line," and "Golden Valley," did not perform as well at the box office. Later, although the company managed to make up for some of the losses with the relatively successful "Daughter's Classic," featuring the entire cast, and "Madam Mai," which had technical shortcomings, it was still far from the path to revival. Lianhua's "Song of the Fishermen" undoubtedly achieved the greatest commercial success this year, but other films such as "The Road to Light," "Iron Bird," "Black Heart Talisman," "Panorama of Southeast Asia," and "Youth" did not perform particularly well at the box office. Tianyi was able to sustain its business because it produced mostly sound films, facing little competition, but this was also due in part to the cleverness of its managers. For example, they were known to produce a film in the shortest possible time with the smallest possible budget. Yihua is a rising star, having released only six films to date: "Rage of the Chinese Sea," "Flames," "The Golden Age," "Woman," "Fairy of the World," and "Flying Flower Village." However, its capital base is quite solid, and "Woman" and "Fairy of the World" were somewhat successful at the box office, so it was perhaps less affected by the economic downturn.

However, the entire Chinese film industry is still struggling. Most companies are adopting austerity policies, and unpaid wages are a common reality. The number of productions is also decreasing step by step, and the trend of cutting corners and producing shoddy work is widespread.

Currently, the film companies' market territory is shrinking day by day, and this has reached a point beyond salvation. Previously, the best overseas markets were the Dutch and British territories in Southeast Asia and Siam, Annam, and the Philippines. Now, the film industry is suffering deeply in these regions, and the livelihood of overseas Chinese is becoming increasingly difficult. Naturally, the film business has plummeted. In the interior, theaters have been affected by the increasing poverty of the society and the impact of exorbitant taxes. Closures due to the inability to afford films are not uncommon. Here, I might as well insert a brief overview of the theater business. Most of the theaters in the cities of the interior are now on the road to closure. For example, in Chengdu, three of the five theaters closed in November of this year, and the remaining two were ordered to close in December by the municipal authorities due to arrears in provincial and municipal medical donations. Of the six theaters in Hankou, only "World" can barely sustain itself, while the rest have either collapsed or are like candles in the wind. The theaters in Guangzhou bear five types of taxes: theater tax, entertainment tax, entertainment stamp tax, advertising tax, and business tax. Unable to bear the burden, they face the risk of complete closure. Even in Shanghai, where there is supposedly gold everywhere, the theater business is not very prosperous. Some first-run theaters have been reduced to second-run theaters, and some have signed exclusive screening rights with film companies for a fixed period. As for internal cost-cutting measures and attempts to save on advertising expenses, these are all in the calculations of theater owners. In such a situation, how can the film companies' market not shrink day by day? Moreover, since the fall of the four northeastern provinces, the vast film market is no longer ours. Even in the war zones and nearby areas, people have little spare money to seek entertainment. How can the film business not plummet?

Due to this situation, film companies have had to make some changes in their film production policies. In the selection of themes, the depiction of the hardships of ordinary people's lives and the powerful exposure of reality will become a way to win cultural and commercial success, and will become the goal of progressive practitioners. On the other hand, the methods of cutting corners and producing shoddy work will inevitably be innovated and diversified. New films featuring the entire cast will become popular, and all kinds of novel and economical methods will be adopted by producers. Although this shows their struggle in distress, it is precisely their step onto the road to self-destruction.

(2) A Glimpse of New Films: This year, Lianhua has released nine productions, Mingxing has released twenty-one, Tianyi has released thirteen, Yihua has released six, and Diantong has released one. In addition, small companies such as Great Wall, Yulian, Tianma, Tianbei, Liangyou, Kuaihuolin, Daguangming, Jinan, Hualun, and Jimei have also produced one or two works each. Among these fewer than one hundred works, there are naturally a few good films, but the number of shoddy and inferior works is at least more than double the number of good films. The works of small companies often imitate successful films made by others. Naturally, some of these imitations are well done, but in general, due to limited manpower and financial resources, their efforts often do not achieve excellent results. What is most inappropriate is that some of them secretly produce martial arts and supernatural films behind closed doors. We don't need to mention that for now. As for the films of the major companies, we don't need to talk about them one by one. Now, I just want to briefly mention a few films that have attracted the attention of the general public. First, I want to talk about "Sister Flowers." "Sister Flowers" is a film that broke the world's box office record by running for two months. Naturally, it has something to satisfy the audience's demands. This is a "bitter drama" without "love" or "sensuality." The reason why it can move the audience is that it allows ordinary people to vent their feelings of distress, that it satirizes reality, and that it embellishes a bit of progressive consciousness. In fact, this work does not have a high degree of technical completion. Both the directing and the performances are partly melodramatic, and this is something that the producers themselves admit.

"Song of the Fishermen" ran for more than eighty days and can be considered the most sensational film of the year. This is also a "bitter drama." It is a source of tears for distressed ordinary people and a refreshing agent for venting their pent-up emotions. Although the author's improved perspective failed to give the audience much healthy feeling, the author's technical cultivation was also able to satisfy the audience and send them home happy.

In addition, Lianhua's "Life," "Wind," "Fragrant Snow Sea," "Goodbye Shanghai," Mingxing's "Salt Tide," "Roadside Willows and Wall Flowers," "Daughter's Classic," "Twenty-Four Hours in Shanghai," "Reborn Flower," Tianyi's "Mr. Wang," "Hundred Flower Island," Yihua's "Rage of the Chinese Sea," "Flames," "Woman," "Fairy of the World," and Diantong's "Peach and Plum Calamity" have all attracted the attention of the general public, but these films cannot be said to be our excellent harvest in 1934. Compared with the massive production and high technical completion of European and American film industries, these films are really insignificant and unworthy of mention.

(3) Several New Trends in Film Production: The Chinese film industry is still very young, but Chinese cinema is not without hope. For example, the progress of Chinese cinema in the past two or three years is undeniable. If Chinese cinema can continue to develop according to the recent situation, it will naturally have a future. However, recently there are indeed many things in the Chinese film industry that cannot but be disappointing. The Chinese film industry has gradually embarked on the wrong path. Due to the sensation of American musical films such as "42nd Street," "Gold Diggers," "Fashions of 1934," and "Wonder Bar," a few Chinese filmmakers are also imitating them, starting to show off sensuality. Following "Fairy of the World," we have the production of films such as "Physical Exercise," "National Beauty and Heavenly Fragrance," and "Song of Roses." This is undoubtedly harmful to the new Chinese cinema. Chinese cinema really has no need to step into the American-style vortex of lasciviousness and depravity again. Secondly, because "Mr. Wang" can make money, envious people then came up with "Goody Goody," "Wine, Women, Wealth, and Temper," "Aviation Saves the Country," etc., and "Mr. Wang's Secret" is also waiting to be produced. Perhaps new tricks will be turned out in the future. But we must know that comedy films are extremely difficult to produce. The current vulgar, boring, opportunistic, and contrived comedies are really not movies, but a waste of movies. Also, the romance films of the Mandarin Duck and Butterfly genre are now showing a tendency to resurface. Tianyi's "Happy Enemies" and "Like Passing Water" are all works of this type, and there are now news that several film companies are taking out these long-shelved film scripts and starting to shoot them again. This is really an unwise act of reversing the trend, because the fact that these films cannot make money has already been proven.

(4) The Flourishing of Film Periodicals: The publication of film periodicals this year can be said to be all the rage. Almost all major newspapers in Shanghai have a film supplement or publish film articles. The Min Bao ("Film Talk") and the Zhonghua Daily ("Ginza") are both newly opened "silver lands" this year. In addition, the Shen Bao ("Film Special Issue"), the Xinwen Bao ("Art Sea"), the Chen Bao ("Daily Film"), the Shishi Xin Bao ("New Shanghai Film Column"), the Shi Bao ("Film Edition"), and the Shanghai Shang Bao ("Silver General Assembly") all specialize in publishing film articles. The evening newspapers, such as the Da Wan Bao ("Silhouette"), ("Sunday Film"), the Da Mei Wan Bao ("Silver Flower"), ("Film Weekly"), the Shi Bao ("Film Journal") ("Weekly"), the Xinwen Ye Bao ("Film Weekly"), the Xin Ye Bao ("Black Eyes") (later renamed "Silver Standard"), and the Shehui Wan Bao ("Film Issue"), are mostly film supplements of their respective newspapers. Stand-alone film publications have also sprung up like mushrooms. This year, we have seen the following monthly magazines: "Film Pictorial," "Era Film," "Modern Film," "Qingqing Film," "Drama and Film," etc. The weekly magazines include "Film Fan Weekly," "Electric Sound," "Film Pictures," etc. The bi-monthly magazines include "Film World," etc. These have all helped to expand the array of film culture to some extent. The film pages in the pictorials are also quite able to arouse people's interest. This year, each pictorial, such as "Liangyou" (recently issued a "Film Special Issue"), "Era," "Art Life," "Greater Shanghai," "China," "Wenhua," "Dazhong," "New Tide," and the rigid "China Monthly," etc., have paid great attention to the publication of film photographs to help people pass the time after tea and dinner. The small newspapers also mostly publish film articles as a gimmick, but most of them only record the daily life of some directors and stars, or promote film companies, or scold people, and are not of much value, but it is not bad to take a look. In short, film has been noticed by a wide audience. Various publications will lose part of their appeal if they do not publish film articles or pictures. It is no wonder that the popularity of film publications has become a recent trend.

(5) Film Criticism and its Future: Now we want to talk about film criticism. This year, the film critics have experienced one storm after another, from the dispute over soft and hard criticism to the discovery of pseudo-experts. After countless battles, large and small, the aftermath has not yet subsided. The reason for this is naturally the shifting of the times, which has drawn a wide chasm of ideological differences. Disputes are unavoidable and very necessary. And this kind of dispute has indeed helped new film criticism. The realism of film criticism and the issue of film criticism standards are constantly raised in the debate, which just exposes the faces of some (technical criticisms) that erase content, some (records) that are close to promoting theaters, or so-called (criticisms) that praise to the sky. However, this has also aroused the jealousy of a few film companies, who have instigated publicists to shout the slogan "No Film Criticism" in an attempt to attack film criticism. Although their plan has not succeeded, the film critics have become more and more motivated, and have tried their best to open up a new and beneficial future for film criticism in the cordial attitude of film criticism writing and in the popularization of film criticism language.

In addition, there are many other major and minor events this year, such as the Nanjing Capital Theater cutting "Daughter's Classic" and restoring "Rape," the film supplements of various newspapers, such as foreign investment in China to film (foreign investment in China to film include the Pudong Sino-Foreign Film Company, the Jiangwan China Film Company, etc.), such as MGM Wah filming "The Good Earth" on location, such as the sensational Xue Yuan (seduction case), Hong Ying's (confession) incident, as well as Ai Xia's suicide, Wang Ying's departure abroad, down to the poor lives of ordinary movie stars, the opening of film companies ...... I can't finish writing, I can't finish talking, so let's stop here.

Chinese Music Over the Past Year

— Wang Daping

Looking at Chinese music over the past year from one perspective, it has made significant progress. However, from another perspective, it also shows its irredeemable decline. There have been many developments in music this year. Now, I will discuss the aspects that show progress and decline.

1. Music in Film

Within its own domain, there isn’t much to mention about music this year. If we are to discuss its progress this year, it would be in its use in films. We all know that talkies are more popular than silent films, but songs, background music, and even sound effects are inseparable from music in talkies. In this context, music is undoubtedly the soul of the film. This year, the music (songs) in domestic talkies, apart from a few songs in films like *Twin Sisters* and *Peach and Plum Calamity*, have largely gone unnoticed. This is naturally due to the poor content and technical quality of the songs. However, the situation changed dramatically with the release of *Fisherman's Song* in the silent film *Song of the Fishermen*. Its sensational impact even created a trend where later films needed music to be successful. Although the composer Ms. An E has said that the success of *Fisherman's Song* was just a "lucky accident," the reality is that the song's realistic content, sorrowful melody, organized composition, and its alignment with the realistic subject matter of the film were all reasons for its sensation. After *Fisherman's Song*, it was a long time before we heard songs like *Graduation Song* from *Peach and Plum Calamity*, *The Road Song*, *Pioneering Song*, *Fengyang Song*, and *Yan Yan Song* from *The Highway*, and *Flying Flower Song* and *Shepherd's Song* from *Flying Flower Village*. Among these, *The Road Song* and *Pioneering Song* are particularly noteworthy for their vigor, novelty, heroism, and pathos. These popular songs should be considered rare productions in the Chinese music scene of 1934.

In addition, there were also some dialogue-singing films from the Star Film Company and Tianyi Film Company, such as *Rebirth Flower*, *Renzhu*, *Red Mansion Spring Deep*, *Spring Night Song*, *Songstress's Scandal*, etc., which also had some songs in them, but these did not attract much attention or have much impact musically.

2. Music in Broadcasting

If broadcasting had no music, it would probably be difficult to attract people's attention and achieve any effect. Most listeners are probably unwilling to listen to educational programs (such as lessons in Mandarin, Chinese studies, English, and primary and secondary school materials) because the material is very dry and not accompanied by music. Drama broadcasts are also unlikely to be effective without good background music. The importance of music in broadcasting can be imagined.

The current state of music broadcasting can be described as shallow, immature, and of little value. The most popular figures in the broadcasting world now are ballad singers, Shanghai opera singers, and female singers. What they broadcast is outdated and harmful. It is impossible to hear anything of value from them. In particular, some of the female announcers only know how to sing a few sentimental popular songs. They do not understand vocal music, and their voices have many flaws. Some of them don't even understand rhythm and beat, let alone anything else. In this state, music has long ceased to exist in the broadcasting world.

Those experts who reside in academies have also gone to the broadcasting stations this year. Students from the National Conservatory of Music had to broadcast a music program once a month in the first half of this year. From the first week of October this year to the first week of June 1935, it was stipulated that music should be broadcast once a week, with the time set from 8:00 PM to 8:45 PM every Friday evening. The programs included ten types: lectures, commemorative programs, music teaching materials, folk songs, art songs, simple art instrumental music, art music, old Chinese music, and new compositions. However, these programs are difficult to attract people's attention among the many bizarre broadcasting programs.

The Shanghai Municipal Council Orchestra also holds broadcasts now. The broadcasting location is at the Westerner’s XOHA radio station, with the time being 9:00 PM to 10:00 PM every other Tuesday evening, and 8:30 PM to 9:30 PM every Friday evening.

In addition, some film songs such as *Fisherman's Song* and *Twin Sisters* are also broadcast a lot, especially *Fisherman's Song*, which has become almost a household name through the broadcasts of various radio stations. This can be said to be a more pleasing thing.

3. Music Concerts

Music concerts are often held in music academies and can be encountered constantly in society. During the summer, the Municipal Council Orchestra often holds performances in various parks in the city. Music experts also occasionally hold music concerts, and students from other schools occasionally come to the city to hold concerts. The Shanghai Municipal Council Symphony Orchestra has always been very famous in the city and holds several music seasons every year. The most recent one started on October 21st, located at the Lyceum Theatre in the French Concession, with the time on Sunday evenings. At the end of November, when the film *Loves of a Musician*, which depicts the love story of the 19th-century musician Schubert, was screened in Shanghai, the orchestra also performed at the venue. The music school holds many concerts. A larger-scale one was the concert held on November 26th to commemorate the school's seventh anniversary, located in the auditorium on the seventh floor of the New Asia Hotel on North Sichuan Road. The performance lasted for four hours, which shows the richness of the program. However, the piano ensemble and Liao Jun's violin solo were particularly unsuccessful in this concert. What was very noticeable in this concert was the Russian composer Tcherepnin's request for submissions of piano pieces with Chinese flavor for a prize. The first prize winner, He Luting, played his work, *The Shepherd's Flute*, in person at the time, which was highly praised by Tcherepnin. In December of this year, the school held another concert of works by teachers and students. This concert also had shortcomings, but there were still many good performances. From this concert, it can be seen that the musicians of the school are working hard on the mixing and harmonization of Chinese and Western music. Chinese music ensembles are also often a program of the school's concerts. This shows a glimpse of the school's efforts.

What must also be mentioned is the performance of Chinese music by the Datong Music Society, which is quite famous in society, on August 27th to commemorate Confucius' birthday. According to experts' criticisms, the performance was a complete failure, and the music played, *Zhonghe Shaoyue*, failed to resonate with the audience. The reason for this can be attributed to the lack of proficiency in performance techniques, the poor quality of the instruments, and the lack of musical value of the music itself (the entire piece of *Zhonghe Shaoyue* is just a simple tune without harmony).

Finally, I have to mention the first record listening session of the "New Voice Society" of the Pathé Records Company in October. This is a listening session for recorded records, not a concert, but I take its similarity and do not want to create a separate title, so I can only talk about it here. The songs we heard this time were *The Road Song*, *Pioneering Song*, *Graduation Song*, and songs from the new opera *Storm on the Dnieper River*. We can hear these songs now. The feeling they give us is very different from some popular songs. There is no decadent music here, only heroism and strength. The lyrics and melody, both in content and form, are very well matched, which cannot be done by a group of people who are good at copying.

4. Music Publishing

In the past year, music publications have not been abundant in quantity, and the quality is even more pitifully poor. In order to promote themselves, film companies have given away the film songs when the films were released, not only directly to the audience but also through bookstores and other institutions to the public. But this does not mean that there is any vitality in the Chinese music publishing industry. In reality, this is just a "business eye" of film companies and theater owners. Mr. Li Jinhui, the most prolific and influential composer in China (whether this influence is good or bad will be discussed later), has also printed quite a few song collections this year. For example, the Tong Sheng Song Collection published by Tong Sheng Bookstore has more than a dozen volumes, with a total of no less than three or four hundred new songs, which can be called a major event. These song collections all have sweet or grand names, such as *Whispers of a Girl*, *Five Dozen Sweet Songs*, *Spring Song in a Small Building*, *Qingfeng Song Collection*, *Humming Collection*, *Roar of the Tiger Mountain*, *Songs of Warriors*, etc. It is said that the content is quite able to cultivate emotions and increase the joy of life, but whether it really has this effect is not something I know.

In addition, many film songs from China and abroad have also been printed and sold by speculators. The ones we are most likely to see are *Twin Sisters* and *Fisherman's Song*, etc. There are also film songs and songs from many years ago printed together in one book, such as *Human Fairy* and *Peach Blossom River*, etc., printed together in one book, which is also often seen. Gao Tianqi and Ma Rouxuan (who has withdrawn) of Tianyi Film Company used the name of the 123 Music Research Association to print a *New Lullaby* this year, printing out the songs from many talkies from Tianyi Film Company from *Spring in the Singing Field* to 1933. Jazz music concerts have also published many jazz music books. In addition, there are inevitably some new songs published, but there is no need to go into detail about them here. As for music theory books, they are even scarcer. We still find it difficult to name a few valuable music books.

In short, the Chinese music publishing industry is still very young and backward. We are not yet able to access valuable music scores and works. This will depend on the efforts of music students.

5. A Brief Record of Musical Debates

At the end of October, an article by Ting Shi, *From Musical Art to China's Pragmatism*, was published in the *Music Weekly* of the *New Evening News*. This immediately attracted the attention of a Mr. Mu Hua in the *Trend* of the *China Daily*, who wrote an article, *Opposing the Poison of an Idealist Applied to Music*, to refute it. Then the two sides began to argue, using pens as swords, stirring up a few rounds of debate. Ting Shi's original opinion was to value the spiritual life of the West. He put forward two requirements: conditional restoration of the old and balancing the spiritual life and material life of the people. Mu Hua pointed out that spiritual life cannot be independent of material life. Under the current economic situation of gradual collapse, the material life of the people cannot be balanced at all. Ting Shi's proposal to balance the material life and spiritual life of the people is not only futile but also harmful. Mu Hua also pointed out Ting Shi's definition of restoration of the old and the confluence of the restoration movement, saying that this is also harmful. Ting Shi later replied that "I want to declare that I have never asked for restoration of the old." In this way, the so-called "restoration of the old" problem has lost its target. Regarding the issue of balancing material life and spiritual life, Ting Shi also declared that he is also dissatisfied with the current material life, but he believes that to transform material life, it is not necessary to start with a frontal reform of material life, but to start with balance. But Mu Hua retorted that this is the result of his not understanding the decisive relationship of material life to spiritual life. In fact, even if he wants to balance, he may not be able to do it.

This debate did not develop well, and the result was only this. Who is right and who is wrong, no third party came out to judge or participate in the discussion later.

6. Prospects for the Future of Music

Although the Chinese music scene in 1934 has not had a bountiful harvest, its bright future has already been foreshadowed. The new shoots of new music will continue to grow, and popular vulgar songs are inevitably about to come to an end. High-level music has gradually attracted the attention of people in society. Popular music, through movies, has gradually been accepted and welcomed by the general public. Although the currently popular vulgar music can still be prominent in the broadcasting and dance circles for a while, this phenomenon is showing that it cannot be maintained for a long time. This can be proved by looking at the two things that even the "ancestors" of the dance circles have organized a "New Song Broadcasting Society" and the music teams of dance halls have degenerated into the same rut. This has fully shown that this kind of thing is just for people to enjoy and has little value.

Speaking of this, the talk is over. Finally, I must declare that I personally do not "care" about music. There may be errors and omissions in what I have said here, and I would like to ask the readers to correct me.

A Week's Trip Back Home (Continued and Finished)

— Su Gang

The boat owner, with a cigarette holder in his mouth, was scolding just like he did on the boat, his eyebrows furrowed and standing up straight like Huang Tianba on the stage. The moment he saw me jump into the water, he hurriedly swam over, his face full of smiles, and said to me, "Sir, I'm really sorry to have made you suffer from the cold... Hey! Look, how can so many big guys be put together in one place? Sir, taking this kind of boat is just not good, you always have to get into the water. Now business is not good, and I don't dare to hire too many boatmen. The boat can't be lifted without the guests getting into the water. Look, more than thirty people can't move it!" His two thick black eyebrows locked into one again, he sighed, and then looked at the dozens of boatmen and scolded them for a while.

The boatmen's faces showed various expressions with the boat owner's scolding, their mouths opening and tilting like river fish. Bamboo poles as thick as bowls were stretched across the front and back of the boat, and more than thirty people were divided into four groups, carrying the boat like a sedan chair. After a tragic shout of "Ah yo yo! Lift yo!", the boat only moved a foot or so.

The few guests in the front cabin, who were happy to see this, hurried over to help the boatmen lift the boat.

The boat owner looked at it and smiled, and said to me, "Sir, haven't you ever done this before? Haha!" He laughed wildly for a while, then put the cigarette holder in his mouth again and sucked it vigorously.

The boat gradually moved away from the bottom of the river, and only the heads of the boatmen were left on the surface of the water. A few boatmen at the front of the boat scrambled to jump on the boat to take the punting poles, and the boat gradually became active.

I jumped onto the boat after them, and felt a bone-chilling coldness all over my body, and shivered immediately. Many boatmen looked at me and laughed and said, "Sir, you're so afraid of the cold, that's terrible! There's a lot more to come ahead!"

"Um!" I responded casually.

I hurriedly put on my clothes and walked out of the cabin, standing at the bow of the boat and looking around for a while. I rarely saw other boats coming and going on the river. Along the river, the fields were full of grass several feet high. As far as I could see, I couldn't see a single village. It was desolate and quiet, which made me think of another world!

I stared blankly for a while, and couldn't help but feel a sense of cursing and sadness!

The boatmen, as if forgetting the fatigue just now, were making a fuss on the bow of the boat in twos and threes. Some were singing love songs from their hometown, and some were sucking on their cigarette holders. The bow of the boat was full of cheerful emotions.

"How much further do we have to go before we have to get into the water again?" I walked to the old boatman and asked.

"Early! If the wind is strong, we will have to get into the water at night. If it doesn't go well, it may be tomorrow morning!" he said while smoking his cigarette.

"What is that beach called ahead? How many more beaches do we have to cross before we get to Guixi?" I asked worriedly.

"That one doesn't have a name, but the shallow places are called 'beaches'. There are still five or six times that the boat will have to be lifted before we get to Guixi. Alas! It's really killing!" he sighed and shook his head.

"That's terrible! There are still so many beaches..."

Before I could finish speaking, he snatched the words and said, "Sir, is that a lot? Hey, if you go to Ganzhou, that's a lot more - Eighteen Beaches! Hey! The water flows so fast there! Eighteen Beaches!"

"It's not easy to be a boatman! Lifting boats, won't that kill people?" I sighed in surprise.

"What can we do? We rely on lifting boats to eat! After we pass Guixi, we don't have to do it anymore. We all go ashore there. We have a life again when the 'fast boats' from Nanchang pass Guixi. Alas! It's not something people do!" He touched his beard twice with his hand, and then said, "From the time I was a child, living to this long beard, I'm still relying on my shoulders to eat in this place. Really, I'm ashamed to death!" Tears flowed from his withered eye sockets.

"Um, it's not easy to eat!" Just as I said this, I heard them shouting for dinner in the cabin. (End)
