Storytelling with Stringed Instruments

Yao Xiao'an Wang Pingqiu Pearl Tower

China and West (1040) 10:00 AM to 11:00 AM

Opening (Shanghai Night)

The spring shade is dark, nearing dusk. Thousands of households light their lamps. Shanghai's prosperity is said to be the greatest. Neon lights illuminate the six streets. One can see the three company rooftops as bright as a painting. The amusement parks are bustling at their peak. The theaters open with a crowd like carps. Reserved boxes are sought until nearly three in the morning. Several Beijing-Suzhou restaurants are just starting banquets. In high spirits, flowers are requested to accompany the guests. Brothel doors compete in extravagance. Red and blue intermingle, clearly distinguishing them. Many wealthy guests support the scene. The sound of trapping sparrows fills the bamboo forest. When the party breaks up, each eats congee. Liu escorts guests, ready to share intimate feelings. Several hotels are enjoying booming business. All rely on the warmth to dispel the cold, using heaters. Even more, the Jai Alai grounds are doing well. Sons and nobles come to bet on wins and losses. Even more, people compete to watch dog racing at Yiyuan. Electric hares fly as dogs chase behind. Dancing prevails in greater Shanghai. Lightly whirling, a paired dance is joyful and resonant. They urge the opening of champagne to kiss each other. Several young people are about to lose their souls. Whispers arrange meetings, emotions seething. To know the value of a spring night is worth a thousand gold. Taking a car home, it's already dawn.

Drama

Guanyin Society

China and West (1040) 7:15 PM to 8:00 PM

(Orchid in the Valley)

Ji Lansun, returning from the battlefield, naturally feels delighted when he arrives in this large and natural countryside. Sad events also arrive quickly: Tao Shijie's father, Tao Xian, and Shijie's younger sister, Renzhu, learn of Shijie's death, which is such a sad thing! And life is contradictory, as Renzhu and Lansun fall in love during this period.

Shen Bao Local Supplement Movie Special

(New Type People) The Reasons Why It's Difficult to Get on Camera (Part Two)

— Ti Yun

The combination of features forms a chimera-like face.

Preconceived notions and audience habits are influenced and shaped.

There is also a very strange thing, which deserves our deeper thought, that is, the easy success of new young actors, from the perspective of (popularity), not necessarily in terms of remuneration, are those few who resemble successful predecessors in appearance. Looking back at the past of the film industry, those who have enjoyed the greatest success and have been supported in the film industry for the longest time, we should first mention Gloria Swanson (GLORIA SWANSON). She voluntarily left the film industry because she wanted to be independent, to be romantic, but if she had not left the film industry, she could still be a dazzling star today. After Swanson left the screen, we had Fay Wray (FAY WRAY). We can say with certainty that Fay's face resembled Swanson's, which at least helped her get an excellent opportunity. When Fay placed her new type of face before film tycoons and audiences, the fact that her face was similar to that of a brilliant film queen was not only harmless to her, but instead helped her success. Perhaps Fay herself did not realize this, but if she examined herself, she would certainly admit that it was an undeniable fact. Of course, after Fay entered the film world, she had to establish her true value, otherwise she would not be able to stand for long in this quicksand-like film world. But Swanson's appearance had already given the audience a pre-emptive statement on her behalf.

Furthermore, when you see Katharine Hepburn (KATHERINE HEPBURN), don't you think of Ms. Garbo (GRETA GARBO)? Wasn't she initially called the American Garbo by the public? If Hepburn is very happy today, and you tell her that her face is very similar to that of the Swedish girl, thus helping her success, she will definitely nod in agreement. But when she is not happy, you mention this, she will get angry and shout: (Who is Garbo? I don't know? Because her wildcat-like temper is like that.

That was still in the silent film era, when Fox was preparing to shoot (Seventh Heaven), nine out of ten general staff members shook their heads when they saw Janet Gaynor (JANET GAYNOR). They didn't know who this new type of girl was, and (Seventh Heaven) was a film with great promise. They suspected that the tycoons in the company were out of their minds, and easily let this unfamiliar person play this important role. They didn't know that the tycoons' vision was very far-reaching. They were sure that Janet Gaynor was a pocket-sized version of Lois Wilson (LOIS WILSON). At that time, Lois Wilson's innocence and naivety represented a pure and flawless woman, which had already been deeply imprinted in the minds of the audience.

Jeanne Eagels' (JEANNE EAGELS) story is very tragic. Her invasion of sound films was because the stage wanted to punish her at that time, and temporarily did not give her work. She brushed her sleeves and went to Hollywood. She starred in a THE LETTER and unexpectedly became famous in one fell swoop. Her unique face and radiant hair felt even more glorious when they appeared on the screen. But it is a pity that she was unable to enjoy her success for a long time, but unconsciously created a ready-made base for Marlene Dietrich (MARLENE DIETRICH). Marlene Dietrich and Jeanne Eagels can be regarded as a pair of sisters. This is not to say that Marlene was hired to come to the United States entirely because she looked like Jeanne Eagels, but we can say that her resemblance to Jeanne Eagels is one of the reasons why we liked her as soon as we saw her.

As for Julie Haydon (JULIE HAYDON), because she looked very much like Ann Harding (ANN HARDING), she played Ann Harding's daughter in the play, thus obtaining an important position, which is especially a fact that everyone knows. At first, the company didn't want Julie to leave any deep traces on Her Private Affair, but afterwards, from the fans' letters, it could be seen that she had already used this step to rise through the ranks, and unexpectedly won a long-term contract with RKO.

Therefore, we feel that the new type of beauties, those who can last on the screen, are still those who wear old masks, those masks that we are already used to seeing. Camera is particularly generous to these types of faces, because these types of faces reflect something incredible, and that incredible thing can only be called illusion (ILLUSION). The correctness of the face, which is what we usually call beauty, rarely makes it onto the camera.

However, whether it is a new type of face, or the old faces that we are used to seeing, they can never be imitated. Specializing in imitating appearances, but lacking substantial content, will be counterproductive. Those who succeed because their faces resemble famous big stars do not rely solely on the similarity of their faces to someone or someone. They must break away from similarities and strive for their own independence and uniqueness. Their resemblance to Swanson, to Garbo, to whoever, to whoever, are all tricks of the camera. But if they don't have their own substantive skills, even if the camera once praised them, they will not be able to maintain their position permanently. (End)

Film Review

Review of (Transatlantic)

— Quan Han

Transatlantic

Merry_Go_Round—Greater Shanghai

Hollywood films, from (1934) onwards, have put on the colorful clothes of song and dance for the usually serious detective films. The development of this trend is undoubtedly based on the popularity of light and lively films.

However, no matter what the form, detective films cannot adopt new content, and will ultimately not be able to save the decline of detective films. That kind of unprincipled description of so-called love disputes between men and women will ultimately not interest people who demand the expression of reality. There is no real content here, only love disputes and pirate elements. Speaking of this, this may conflict with Hollywood's cleanliness movement, and films that are sexually suggestive or promote theft are classified as being cleared by gentlemen. However, from a new perspective, as long as the author originally produced it to expose reality, and its effect is not to obtain the opposite effect of being sexually suggestive or promoting theft, then taking sex and theft as the subject matter is definitely not moral depravity. On the contrary, in the sense of expressing reality, it will have its great success. However, this requirement is not easily accepted by American film writers.

What is expressed in (Transatlantic)? How does the director express it? Here are gorgeous songs and dances, enchanting love songs, and flirtations. Gambling and clever tricks of stealing, these all make people seeking entertainment feel some interest.

In addition, we can't find anything particularly worth learning in this film. It's good to give the audience happiness and joy in this new year.

There are Three Kinds of National Flags in (Eternal Love)

— Lian

I don't know where this news came from, saying that Fei Mu left Lianhua to join another company. Although this matter has not been confirmed for many days, there are still outsiders who are skeptical. Therefore, those who care about Lianhua and love Fei Mu have recently sent letters asking about this matter. From this point of view, Fei Mu is indeed of great importance in Lianhua, and it can also be said in the Chinese film industry. However, rumors are rumors, and facts are facts. The fact is that (Eternal Love), which he co-directed with Luo Mingyou, has indeed started filming. Here is also a great thing to report to everyone, that there are three kinds of national flags in (Eternal Love). Everyone thinks, a film uses three kinds of national flags, you say is it great enough? At this time, Fei Mu, seeing this manuscript being written by the side, couldn't help but smile and say: (It's a pity that there are only three kinds of national flags here, if there were all the flags of the world, it would be even greater!) Those who heard it praised Lao Fei for his humor.

New Star Films in 1935

— Huo

In 1935, the new films that the Star Company is eager to release or are in production include the following:

(Orchid in the Valley) is directed by Zhang Shichuan, and stars Hu Die and Gao Zhanfei. This film was originally Star's silent film, and its content is as (full of twists and turns) and (sad and stubborn) as possible. This time it has been changed to a sound film, so of course this silent film is even more spectacular.

(Falling Flowers Season) is Wu Cun's second masterpiece after Remarriage. The theme depicts a group of volunteers and a young girl who wandered to Shanghai and ate up the pain of life. From (Falling Flowers Season) to (Heavy Snow), the winter is used to express a very sad mood. The picture is as beautiful as a poem, overflowing with the spirit of (joy) and (sorrow).

(Human Relations) is directed by Li Pingqian, and stars Gong Jianong, Zheng Xiaoqiu, and Zhu Qiuhen. It depicts the tragic experience of a young man growing old, how he becomes unemployed, how his wife and children are scattered, and how he is unfortunately imprisoned. This is a film similar to Paul Muni's (I Am a Fugitive from a Chain Gang).

(Tuberose) (Boat Girl) (Night Meeting) are all sound films. The three all depict the darkness, sin, economic collapse, and rural bankruptcy of the city. In this stormy era, films of this kind undoubtedly have important significance. The directors are Cheng Bugao, Shen Xiling, and Yao Sufeng.

There are also (Beauty's Heart), which was filmed a year ago, and the temporarily shelved Nostalgia. (Rebirth Flower) (24 Hours in Shanghai) etc. are being screened in the New Light and Central Theaters. (But)

Moving Towards (The Big Road) in 1935

— Songhua

The first thing that Xingguo people came into contact with on New Year's Day in 1935 was the Lianhua Film Company's (The Big Road), which was being screened at Jincheng. Perhaps this is a symbol of the new China moving towards (The Big Road)? Let us wish it in advance!

(The Big Road) is Lianhua Company's all-out production. In terms of its significance, director, and actors, it really has a value that surpasses everything. Therefore, during the production period, (The Big Road) had already established solid expectations and faith in society. And the (The Big Road) that has now been built will of course live up to the expectations of the Chinese people.

In terms of significance, (The Big Road) truly expresses the greatness of the Chinese people's united strength. In China, where imperialism and local bullies collude to oppress each other, the method of self-rescue depends only on its own unity and efforts. There is no doubt that in the film, the local bullies used various methods to destroy the people's front, but due to the consolidation of the people's internal affairs, they finally failed. This, on the one hand, exposes the ugliness of the collusion between imperialism and evil forces, and on the other hand, shows that the people's power cannot be insulted. The seriousness of its significance and the reality of its subject matter are undoubtedly the films that China urgently needs today.

The director of this film is Sun Yu, who revived national films. Based on his past contributions to the Chinese film scene, we can of course trust him. The actors are led by Jin Yan, and twelve stars including Chen Yan Yan, Li Lili, Zhang Yi, and Luo Ming are gathered to co-star. Lianhua's male stars have all been gathered in this film. The performance is both tragic and humorous, and grabs the audience's emotions everywhere. The plot is strong and unprecedented. It is indeed a film worthy of movie fans' attention.

Special New Year's Issue of Electric Sound Weekly

Electric Sound Film Picture Weekly. In order to celebrate the New Year's Day of the 24th year of the Republic of China and thank the readers who love it, a special New Year's issue is published. The content is wonderful and includes twelve more pages of copper illustrations and text. The photos published are extremely valuable, and many are specially taken. In particular, the photos of star couples such as (Ruan Lingyu and Tang Jishan), (Hu Die and Pan Yousheng), and (Chen Yan Yan and Wang Shaofen) are the most valuable. As for the text, there are multiple sections such as (Chronicle of Major Film Events in the 23rd Year of the Republic of China) (Dumping of Hollywood Bastards) (Cigarette Queen Hu Die Touches a Bad Omen) and (Secrets of Female Stars' Private Lives), which cannot be explored from the outside. Each volume sells for one dime and is attached with a large sheet of broadcasting weekly newspaper. It has been published on New Year's Day. All major bookstores and newsstands have it for sale. The general distribution is Sanhe Publishing House, No. 54 Nanjing Road, Shanghai.

Movie Novels

Police Romance (White Lies) (2)

— Xin Zhi

Qiong was taking a bath in the tub. While splashing water, she was wondering how to meet this Tyler Camden. She was picturing in her mind what kind of person this bold policeman was. Was he tall? Was his complexion dark? Was he thin? Was his hair red? Did his eyes smile before he spoke? She clearly knew that she was engaged to Axel Brantley. She was even going out with him tonight. But she couldn't make up her mind whether her heart would change once she met this Tyler.

At this moment, Mitchell was sitting in his study, excitedly reading a news proof, having completely forgotten everything from before. Because the news he had in his hand now was a sensational piece, exclusive to his Express. That news was extremely convoluted and moving, capable of bringing tears to one's eyes. It turned out that a senior bank employee, named Dan Oliver, had embezzled 30,000 yuan from the bank several years ago. But after embezzling it, he deeply regretted it and wanted to gradually repay it. He had already put back most of it, leaving only about 10,000 yuan, but his actions had been discovered. A reporter for the Express, named Roberts, was the first to know about this. But he had promised Oliver not to disclose the news, because Oliver pleaded bitterly, giving him a chance to reform, and he was already deeply repentant. Roberts was a soft-hearted person and readily agreed to keep the secret for him. However, Mitchell refused. He said that was not how he cultivated his newspaper. He said he only had one policy: to get news, get it fast, get it right! He didn't care about anything else! Whoever runs into it, whoever is unlucky, as long as there is no room for them to sue him! Take this Dan Oliver, for example. He did something wrong and committed a crime. Those are all facts. Therefore, he, Mitchell, could loudly announce his criminal past, word for word, in his newspaper. In this way, everyone would rush to buy the Express to read. That was a legitimate way to promote newspaper sales. As for Dan Oliver, he was just a legitimate unlucky guy, who deserved to be used by him.

The next morning, when he took his big car to his newspaper office, he felt happy thinking about his upcoming victory. He seemed to already hear the printing press in the machine room, rotating with a rumbling sound. He also seemed to hear the newsboys on the streets, raising their voices to call out. He also seemed to hear the noisy discussions on the streets about this shocking case, and he also seemed to hear everyone praising how well-informed the Express was, a place that other newspapers could not reach. When his car entered the bustling city and drove through the noisy crowd, he thought of his daughter again, wondering what she was doing now. Perhaps she was having her sweet spring dream, this little devil. He couldn't help but chuckle. His daughter and a police officer. If she hadn't pleaded for him, that policeman would probably be wandering the streets now.

Soon he arrived at the Express's newspaper office. The staff were bustling about, extremely busy. The sound of typewriters, the sound of telephone bells, the sound of conversations, and the sound of the printing presses in the basement, all mixed together, created a scene of a thriving newspaper business. Mitchell nodded to everyone as he walked along. He walked into his private office. He briefly reviewed the routine matters and ordered the local news editor to be invited. Soon the local news editor arrived, and he instructed: (Move everything else away and put this Dan Oliver case on the front page. There are still many changes to be made in these proofs. First, the line of text below the copperplate should be changed to (Dan Oliver, senior bank employee, arrested for embezzlement). The rest, I have written, you can read it yourself.) The chief editor agreed repeatedly and walked out. Mitchell was still shouting from behind: (Hurry up! My newspaper will be on the streets in thirty minutes!) (To be continued)
